        <g id="chapter-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring" transform="translate(840.000000, 0.000000)">
            <g id="Bread-Crumb-&gt;-Title" transform="translate(-1.000000, 57.000000)">
                <g id="Group-4">
                    <g id="Group-2">
                        <rect id="Rectangle" stroke="#FFFFFF" fill="#FFFFFF" x="0.5" y="0.5" width="319" height="46" rx="8"></rect>
                        <text id="1.-Recruiting-and-hi" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="14" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.105000004" fill="#000000">
                            <tspan x="20" y="32">1. Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                        </text>
                    </g>
                    <text id="Federal-Human-Resour" font-family="Helvetica" font-size="6" font-weight="normal" letter-spacing="0.0450000018" fill="#000000">
                        <tspan x="20" y="12">Federal Human Resources Manual / Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                    </text>
                </g>
                <line x1="0.5" y1="46.5" x2="320.5" y2="46.5" id="Line" stroke="#979797" stroke-width="0.5" stroke-linecap="square"></line>
            </g>
            <text id="Text-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="12" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.0900000036" fill="#000000">
                <tspan x="39" y="132">Verification of employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="146" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="160" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Federal law</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="174" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="188" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The Immigration Reform and Control </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="202" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Act¬†(IRCA) requires employers to employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="216" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">only those persons authorized to work in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="230" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this country. Employers are required to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="244" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verify¬†the identity and employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="258" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of all individuals hired after November 6, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="272" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">1986, regardless of how many people the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="286" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company employs. Verification of identity </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="300" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and employment eligibility is accomplished </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="314" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by completing Form I-9. An employer should </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="328" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be careful not to engage in document abuse </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="342" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrimination in this process by specifying </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="356" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">what documents the employee presents, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="370" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requiring more documents than are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="384" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">minimally necessary or rejecting documents </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="398" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that reasonably appear to be genuine.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="412" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="426" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should keep I-9 forms for at least </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="440" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">three years from the date of hire and for one </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="454" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year from the date employment terminates. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="468" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once an employer is certain they have met </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="482" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">both tests, the forms should be thrown </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="496" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">away. An employer is allowed to make </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="510" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies of the documents presented by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="524" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employee, but they must still complete </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="538" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the form also. Under present regulations, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="552" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the retention rules do not apply to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="566" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="580" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="594" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee presents a work </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="608" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document with an expiration </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="622" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">date, the employer must reverify </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="636" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment eligibility before that document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="650" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">expires. Reverification is accomplished by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="664" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">examining a new document and completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="678" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Section 3 of the I-9 form. Employers do not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="692" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need to reverify U.S. passports and I-551 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="706" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Permanent Resident or Resident </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="720" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrant) cards.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="734" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="748" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee cannot present an original </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="762" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document for employment eligibility, an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="776" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer may accept a receipt for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="790" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">replacement employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="804" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document. The receipt will allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="818" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment for 90 days from the date of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="832" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receipt or the date the prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="846" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization expired, whichever is later. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="860" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Remember that the employer will need to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="874" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reverify employment eligibility at the end of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="888" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the 90-day ‚Äúgrace‚Äù period.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="902" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="916" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Note: Employers cannot accept receipts if </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="930" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employment will last three days or less.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="944" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="958" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The government must give three-days‚Äô </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="972" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">notice in writing before inspecting I-9 forms. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="986" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should use this time wisely to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1000" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">ensure that their forms are correctly </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1014" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">completed and that they have all the forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1028" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that should be retained. As a general rule, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1042" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employers should politely insist upon their </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1056" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">right to advance notice of an audit and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1070" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">should not waive their rights by agreeing to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1084" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an inspection of only a handful of forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1098" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1112" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1126">No match letters</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1140" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1154" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">As of September 14, 2007, Immigration and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1168" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Customs Enforcement¬†(ICE) has changed </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1182" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the regulations relating to the unlawful hiring </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1196" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or continued employment of unauthorized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1210" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants. The amended regulations apply </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1224" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the employment verification process and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1238" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">impose new obligations on employers when </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1252" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an employer either:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1266" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1280" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a ‚Äúno match‚Äù letter from the Social </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1294" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Security Administration</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1308" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a letter regarding employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1322" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verification forms from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1336" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1350" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The new regulation has been criticized by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1364" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">some as a back-door way for the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1378" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government to address the nation‚Äôs growing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1392" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal immigration population in the wake of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1406" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">repeated failures by Congress to pass a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1420" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">comprehensive immigration reform bill.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1434" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1448" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the new regulation, employers have a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1462" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">heightened duty to follow up on no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1476" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">letters and other employment verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1490" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancies. The Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1504" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security takes the position that a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1518" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no-match letter is a distinct indication that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1532" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the subject employee is not authorized to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1546" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in the United States. The regulation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1560" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">creates an expansive definition of the term </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1574" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúconstructive knowledge‚Äù as applied to an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1588" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs information about an individual‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1602" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work in the United States </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1616" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the Immigration and Nationality Act.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1630" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1644" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An employer may violate federal regulations </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1658" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">if it has knowledge that an employee is an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1672" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker. An employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1686" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">deemed to have knowledge if a reasonable </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1700" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person would infer from the facts that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1714" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee is unauthorized. Constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1728" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge can be found where one of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1742" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following is true:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1756" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1770" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The I-9 form employment eligibility form has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1784" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not been properly completed (including </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1798" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">support documentation).</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1812" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer has learned that the worker is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1826" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not authorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1840" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1854" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer acts with reckless disregard </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1868" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for the legal consequences or permitting </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1882" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">another individual to introduce an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1896" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker into the workforce.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1910" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Examples of an employer‚Äôs constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1924" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge that an employee may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1938" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work include:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1952" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1966" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Social Security </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1980" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Administration that the combination of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1994" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">name and social security number submitted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2008" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for an employee do not match agency </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2022" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2036" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2050" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security that the immigration </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2064" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status document or employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2078" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document presented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2092" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referenced by the employee in completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2106" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9 was assigned to another person or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2120" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the agency has no record that the document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2134" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has been assigned</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2148" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a request by a worker (who already claimed </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2162" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to be a permanent resident, U.S. citizen or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2176" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. national) that the employer file an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2190" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant labor certification or employment-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2204" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">based immigration visa petition.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2218" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The amended regulation also describes </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2232" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúsafe harbor‚Äù procedures that the employer </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2246" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">can follow in response to such a letter and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2260" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">thereby be certain that the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2274" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security will not use the letter as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2288" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">part of an allegation that the employer had </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2302" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">constructive knowledge that the employee </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2316" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referred to in the letter is an immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2330" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2344" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.¬† The ‚Äúsafe harbor‚Äù procedures </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2358" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">include attempting to resolve the no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2372" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">issue and, if it cannot be resolved within a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2386" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certain period of time, independently </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2400" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verifying the employee‚Äôs identity and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2414" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment authorization through a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2428" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialized process.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2442" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2456" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigration and Customs Enforcement </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2470" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">considers employers to have acted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2484" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reasonably if the employer resolves the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2498" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancy with the relevant agency within </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2512" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">30 days of receiving a no match letter by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2526" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">doing all of the following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2540" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2554" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">checking its records for a clerical error</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2568" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">informing the agency of its error</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2582" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verifying that the name and number, as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2596" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">corrected, match the agency‚Äôs records.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2610" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employer cannot resolve the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2624" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancy as described above, it must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2638" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">contact the employee and request </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2652" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">confirmation that the employee‚Äôs information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2666" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is correct. If the original information was </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2680" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct, the employer must do all of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2694" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2708" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2722" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct the employee‚Äôs information in its </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2736" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2750" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">inform the relevant agency of the correction</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2764" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">match the corrected information with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2778" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">agency‚Äôs records.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2792" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee who is the subject of a no-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2806" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">match letter maintains that the information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2820" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">he or she provided to the employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2834" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct, the employer must ask the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2848" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee to pursue the matter him or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2862" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">herself with the agency. Employers who </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2876" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">take these corrective steps within 30 days of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2890" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receiving a no-match letter are regarded as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2904" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">having acted reasonably and fall within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2918" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">safe-harbor.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2932" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2946" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Likewise, many states have laws making it </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2960" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal for an employer to knowingly employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2974" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or refer for employment any individual who </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2988" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has illegally entered the United States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3002" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3016">Temporary visas</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3030" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3044" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. employers may sponsor foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3058" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employees for certain temporary </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3072" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa¬†categories that authorize employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3086" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in this country. Some of these categories </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3100" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">include:¬†</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3114" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3128" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B ‚Äì Specialty occupation (professional)</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3142" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3156" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B visa is for professionals who will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3170" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in a ‚Äúspecialty occupation‚Äù on a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3184" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary basis for no more than six years. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3198" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The duration of stay is three years, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3212" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">extendable to six years. An exception to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3226" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">maximum length of stay applies in certain </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3240" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">circumstances. A specialty occupation is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3254" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">one that requires:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3268" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3282" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">theoretical and practical application of a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3296" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">body of highly specialized knowledge</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3310" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">attainment of a bachelor‚Äôs or higher degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3324" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in the specific specialty (or its equivalent) as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3338" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a minimum for entry into the occupation in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3352" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3366" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are numerous occupations that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3380" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">potentially qualify as specialty occupations. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3394" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer must prove -- through </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3408" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">objective evidence -- that the job offered </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3422" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">falls within the statutory and regulatory </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3436" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">definitions set forth.¬† Typical occupations </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3450" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualifying for H1B visa status include </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3464" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professions, which are defined by INA </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3478" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬ß101(a)(32) to include architects, engineers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3492" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">lawyers, physicians, surgeons and teachers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3506" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in elementary or secondary schools, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3520" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">colleges, academies or seminaries. H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3534" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visas are employer and job specific.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3548" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3562" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Current laws limit the annual number of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3576" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualifying foreign workers who may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3590" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">issued a visa or otherwise be provided H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3604" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status to 65,000 with an additional 20,000 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3618" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the H-1B advanced degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3632" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">exemption.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3646" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3660" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B1 (Chile and Singapore) program </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3674" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">allows employers to temporarily employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3688" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign workers from Chile and Singapore in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3702" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States on a nonimmigrant basis </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3716" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in specialty occupations. Current laws limit </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3730" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the annual number of qualifying foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3744" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">workers who may be issued an H-1B1 visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3758" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to 6,800 with 1,400 from Chile and 5,400 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3772" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">from Singapore.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3786" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3800" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B petition process involves </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3814" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certification of a labor condition </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3828" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">application¬†(LCA) by the U.S. Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3842" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Labor (DOL) and approval of an H-1B visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3856" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition filed with the USCIS. Employers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3870" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must submit an LCA to the DOL </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3884" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">electronically through the FLAG system </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3898" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">attesting to compliance with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3912" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirements of H-1B or H-1B1. LCAs must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3926" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not be submitted more than six months </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3940" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before the beginning date of the period of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3954" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment. The two exceptions to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3968" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">electronic filing are employers with physical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3982" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">disabilities or those who lack Internet </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3996" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">access and cannot electronically file the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4010" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form ETA-9035E. An employer must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4024" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition the administrator of OFLC for prior </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4038" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">special permission to file an LCA by mail on </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4052" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the Form ETA-9035.¬† After the employer‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4066" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B petition is approved by USCIS, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4080" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">individual worker can obtain an H-1B visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4094" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">stamp by appointment at the U.S. consulate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4108" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or embassy in his or her native country. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4122" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the individual is already in the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4136" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States, a change of status to H-1B is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4150" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">possible; and if the individual is already in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4164" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B status, he or she can begin working </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4178" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for a new H-1B employer as soon as the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4192" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs petition is filed without having to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4206" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">wait for an approval. The LCA verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4220" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">process requires the employer to certify that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4234" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4248" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4262" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B individual will be paid the higher of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4276" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">prevailing or actual wage for that occupation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4290" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in the area of intended employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4304" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will offer the individual the same </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4318" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">terms and conditions of employment that it </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4332" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offers to U.S. workers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4346" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment of the noncitizen will not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4360" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">adversely affect the wages and working </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4374" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">conditions of workers similarly employed in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4388" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the area of intended employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4402" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will not employ the individual in a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4416" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">strike or lockout or work stoppage related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4430" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a labor dispute in the occupation at the time </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4444" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the application is signed</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4458" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will notify other similarly situated </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4472" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employees (or their agent) of its intent to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4486" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employ an H-1B individual in the relevant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4500" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">position.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4514" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer must also document its </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4528" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">compliance with the LCA verifications by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4542" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">retaining relevant documents and by making </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4556" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available a ‚Äúpublic inspection‚Äù file upon </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4570" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">request.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4584" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4598" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B status is initially granted for no more </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4612" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">than three years. Extensions are available, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4626" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">but the employee is subject to a maximum </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4640" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">cumulative period of six years of H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4654" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status. H-1B extensions beyond the six-year </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4668" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">limit are possible if the individual is the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4682" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">beneficiary of an employment-based </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4696" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence process that has been </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4710" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">pending for more than one year or is the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4724" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">beneficiary of an approved immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4738" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition and is unable to adjust status to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4752" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence because of per-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4766" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country limits.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4780" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4794" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer will be liable for the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4808" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reasonable costs of the foreign national's </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4822" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">return transportation if the employer </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4836" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">terminates the foreign national before the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4850" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">end of the foreign national's period of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4864" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorized stay. The employer is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4878" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">responsible for the costs of foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4892" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">national's return transportation if foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4906" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">national voluntarily resigns the position.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4920" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4934" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Treaty NAFTA ‚Äì Canadian and Mexican </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4948" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professionals</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4962" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4976" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the North American Free Trade </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4990" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Agreement¬†(NAFTA), citizens of Canada </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5004" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and Mexico who are qualified professionals </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5018" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">can work in the United States using the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5032" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Treaty NAFTA or TN, classification. This </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5046" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa category is available for designated </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5060" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professional occupations set forth in an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5074" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">appendix to NAFTA. The list of professions </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5088" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">includes many occupations that would also </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5102" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualify for H-1 status, such as engineers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5116" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">accountants and professors. One advantage </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5130" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of TN status is that the application </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5144" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure is very simple. An applicant can </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5158" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">apply at the border by presenting all of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5172" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5186" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5200" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">proof of Canadian or Mexican citizenship</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5214" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">proof of membership in a listed occupation</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5228" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an offer of employment in that occupation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5242" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">from a U.S. employer</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5256" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$50.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5270" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The ‚Äúapplication‚Äù is adjudicated on-the-spot </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5284" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and, if approved, the immigrant is given a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5298" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">multiple-entry TN status good for one year.¬†¬†</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5312" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5326" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Although TN status can theoretically be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5340" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">renewed indefinitely in one-year increments </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5354" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a petition or by reapplying at the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5368" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">border, in practice the status may be limited </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5382" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to five or six years of renewals because the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5396" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">treaty states that TN status cannot be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5410" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted to an immigrant who intends to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5424" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reside in the United States permanently. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5438" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of TN immigrants can get TD </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5452" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Treaty Dependent) status but cannot use </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5466" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that status to work in this country.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5480" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5494" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1A and L-1B ‚Äì Intracompany transfers of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5508" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managers/executives or specialized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5522" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge personnel</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5536" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5550" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The L-1A¬†and L-1B visas are designed to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5564" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">facilitate the temporary transfer of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5578" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managerial, executive and specialized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5592" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge personnel from overseas entities </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5606" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to related U.S. entities. L-1A status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5620" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managers and executives and L-1B status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5634" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for persons with specialized knowledge of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5648" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company methods, products, procedures, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5662" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">operations, etc. To qualify for L-1 status, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5676" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee must have worked for the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5690" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company abroad in a managerial, executive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5704" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or specialized knowledge position for at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5718" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">least one full year during the three years </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5732" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">prior to the transfer to a managerial, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5746" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executive or specialized knowledge position </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5760" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">with the related U.S. entity. First line </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5774" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">supervisors are not eligible for L-1A status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5788" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">as managers unless the persons they </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5802" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">supervise are professionals.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5816" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5830" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The U.S. employer must file a petition for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5844" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1 status with the regional USCIS Service </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5858" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Center with jurisdiction over the location </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5872" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">where the immigrant will work. Canadian </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5886" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferees may submit the petition at the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5900" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S.-Canada border for immediate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5914" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">adjudication. Once the employer‚Äôs petition is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5928" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">approved, the immigrant may obtain an L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5942" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa stamp from the U.S. embassy or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5956" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">consulate abroad or if already in the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5970" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States, may commence the L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5984" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5998" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6012" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1 status is initially granted for three years </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6026" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and extensions are available for two-year </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6040" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">periods. L-1A managers/executives are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6054" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entitled to up to seven years of L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6068" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment in the United States and L-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6082" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialized knowledge personnel are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6096" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">eligible for a maximum of five years of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6110" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorized stay. Dependents of L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6124" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferees obtain L-2 status. Unlike most </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6138" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary visa categories that do not allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6152" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependents to work, L-2 spouses may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6166" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">obtain employment authorization.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6180" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6194" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Some multi-national companies may qualify </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6208" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for ‚Äúblanket‚Äù L-1 status. Typically, this is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6222" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available for entities that transfer more than </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6236" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">10 people per year, have annual sales in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6250" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">excess of $25 million or more than 1,000 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6264" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. employees. Blanket L-1 status allows </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6278" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. entity to bypass the USCIS petition </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6292" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">process in individual cases. Instead, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6306" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. entity sends a special form to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6320" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferee, who then applies for L-1 status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6334" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">directly at the U.S. consulate or embassy.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6348" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6362" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1 and E-2 ‚Äì Treaty trader/investor</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6376" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6390" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Based upon a bilateral investment treaty or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6404" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a treaty of friendship, navigation and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6418" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commerce between the United States and a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6432" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign country, an individual may come to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6446" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States to open and operate a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6460" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign-owned business or be employed in a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6474" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign-owned business that already exists </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6488" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">here. Entities engaged in substantial trade </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6502" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">between the United States and the treaty </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6516" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country will be able to transfer managers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6530" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives and key personnel using the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6544" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1¬†(Treaty Trader) visa status. Entities </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6558" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">making a substantial investment in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6572" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States may transfer managers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6586" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives and key personnel using the E-2 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6600" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Treaty Investor) visa status.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6614" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6628" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The foreign entity must be a ‚Äúcitizen‚Äù or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6642" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúnative‚Äù of the treaty country. This means </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6656" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that at least a majority of the ownership of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6670" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the foreign entity must be held by citizens of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6684" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the treaty country. The person seeking E </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6698" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa status must also be a citizen of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6712" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">treaty country. There is no prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6726" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirement, however.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6740" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6754" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1 immigrants must be engaged in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6768" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">activities supporting a substantial volume of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6782" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">international trade in goods or services. E-2 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6796" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants must be directing or developing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6810" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an active and substantial investment of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6824" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">irrevocably committed funds devoted to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6838" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">production of goods or services. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6852" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚ÄúSubstantial‚Äù means more than enough to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6866" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">secure the success of the enterprise and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6880" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">more than enough to support the E </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6894" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant and family members.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6908" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6922" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Most E immigrants apply for E visa status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6936" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">directly at the U.S. embassy or consulate in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6950" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the treaty country, but it is possible to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6964" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">change to E status from within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6978" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States Immigrants admitted in E status are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6992" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted two years of authorized stay so long </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7006" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">as their E visa stamp is valid at the time of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7020" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entry. Typically, E visas are valid for five </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7034" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">years, but this may vary depending upon </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7048" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the terms of the treaty. In most cases, the E </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7062" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa can be renewed for additional periods </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7076" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">provided that the underlying trade or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7090" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">investment remains viable.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7104" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7118" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of E visa immigrants acquire </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7132" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the same status as the principal immigrant, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7146" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">such as E-1 or E-2 status. E-2 spouses may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7160" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">obtain employment authorization.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7174" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7188" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2A and H-2B ‚Äì Agricultural and other </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7202" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">seasonal and temporary workers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7216" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7230" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-2A visa¬†is for seasonal agricultural </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7244" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">workers and the H-2B visa¬†is for non-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7258" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">agricultural temporary or seasonal workers. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7272" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2 status is only available for jobs that are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7286" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">truly temporary in nature, so the status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7300" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">almost always limited to one year. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7314" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer must test the market for available </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7328" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. workers and obtain a certification from </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7342" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">DOL that none are available to fill the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7356" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary position(s). The test of the market </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7370" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must offer prevailing wages and working </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7384" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">conditions.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7398" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7412" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There is a quota or limit on the number of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7426" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2B visas that can be issued each fiscal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7440" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year. Often, the quota is exhausted well </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7454" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before the end of the fiscal year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7468" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7482" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2A employers may be required to hire </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7496" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. workers who apply for work anytime up </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7510" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to halfway through the certification period, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7524" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">even if that involves discharging the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7538" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant worker. Also, H-2A employers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7552" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">may need to pay special wages, offer </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7566" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">housing and in some cases may have to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7580" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">pay transportation costs for the immigrant to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7594" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">come to the work site and return home.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7608" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7622" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Each H-2 period of authorized stay will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7636" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">one year or less. After using three </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7650" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">consecutive H-2 periods, the immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7664" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must remain outside the United States for at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7678" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">least six months before becoming eligible to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7692" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">use H-2 status again.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7706" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7720" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-3 ‚ÄìTrainees</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7734" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7748" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">A U.S. employer may sponsor an immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7762" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for H-3¬†status to provide the immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7776" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training that is unavailable in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7790" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs native country. The immigrant is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7804" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not supposed to engage in productive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7818" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training other than as necessary to provide </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7832" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">effective training. H-3 immigrants cannot </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7846" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">displace U.S. workers. The petitioning </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7860" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer must supply extensive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7874" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">documentation of an appropriate training </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7888" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">curriculum with the petition. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7902" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">documentation must specifically discuss the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7916" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">amount of on-the-job vs. classroom training, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7930" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">address why the training is not available in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7944" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the trainee‚Äôs native country and explain how </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7958" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the training experience will enhance the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7972" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs career prospects abroad. H-3 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7986" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status is limited to the duration of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8000" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training program, which cannot exceed two </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8014" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">years.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8028" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8042" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-1 ‚ÄìAcademic students</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8056" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8070" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-l visas¬†are for students engaged in degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8084" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">programs at U.S. academic institutions. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8098" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are several types of employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8112" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization available to F-l foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8126" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">students, including on-campus employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8140" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">off-campus employment due to severe </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8154" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">economic hardship, international </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8168" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">organization internships, curricular practical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8182" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training and optional practical training </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8196" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before and after completion of studies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8210" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8224" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An F-l student engaged in a full course of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8238" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">study may engage in part-time on-campus </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8252" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment such as working in a cafeteria </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8266" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or bookstore so long as this employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8280" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">does not displace a U.S. worker. This type </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8294" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of on-campus employment does not require </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8308" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">advance permission from USCIS.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8322" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8336" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An F-l student may apply for employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8350" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work off-campus due to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8364" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">economic necessity or for an internship with </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8378" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an international organization. Economic </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8392" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">necessity work permits are normally not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8406" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted except upon proof of a substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8420" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and unforeseen change in the student‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8434" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">finances.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8448" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8462" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-1 students may also engage in practical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8476" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training employment related to their degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8490" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">program. While enrolled, F-1 students may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8504" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">use Curricular Practical Training. This may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8518" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">take the form of an internship, co-op, work-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8532" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">study program or some other activity that is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8546" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an integral part of the degree program and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8560" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">CPT can be commenced upon an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8574" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">endorsement by the school‚Äôs foreign student </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8588" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">advisor. A student who uses more than 12 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8602" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">months of CPT becomes ineligible for post-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8616" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">graduate Optional Practical Training¬†(OPT).</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8630" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8644" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">OPT permits up to 12 months of on-the-job </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8658" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">practical training upon completion of an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8672" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">academic degree program. F-1 students </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8686" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must apply for a work permit in order to use </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8700" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">OPT and cannot commence employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8714" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">until the permit is issued.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8728" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
