                <tspan x="39" y="8742" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of F-1 immigrants are granted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8756" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-2 status and cannot work.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8770" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8784" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">J-1 ‚ÄìExchange visitors</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8798" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8812" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrants participating in a designated </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8826" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">exchange visitor program may engage in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8840" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specific types of employment as part of their </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8854" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">program activities. There are many types of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8868" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">J-1 exchange visitor programs, including </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8882" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">those for students, practical trainees, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8896" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">teachers, professors, research assistants, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8910" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialists, camp counselors, au pairs and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8924" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">distinguished visitors. J-1 practical trainees </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8938" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">are authorized up to 18 months of on-the-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8952" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">job training; other categories have different </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8966" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">time limits.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8980" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8994" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Some exchange visitors are subject to a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9008" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">two-year home country residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9022" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirement that must be satisfied before </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9036" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant is eligible for H, L or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9050" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent resident status. This obligation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9064" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">arises if the immigrant‚Äôs exchange visit is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9078" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">funded by the immigrant‚Äôs government or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9092" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. government, if the immigrant‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9106" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">skills are in short supply in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9120" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country or if the immigrant is coming to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9134" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States to obtain graduate medical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9148" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">education. If the immigrant is subject to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9162" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">two-year residence requirement, so too are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9176" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">all of the immigrant‚Äôs dependents. It is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9190" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sometimes possible to obtain a waiver of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9204" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this requirement, but the waiver process is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9218" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">cumbersome and time-consuming.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9232" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9246" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">O ‚ÄìExtraordinary ability immigrants</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9260" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9274" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The O category is for highly talented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9288" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">acclaimed individuals who are scientists, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9302" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">educators, artists, athletes, entertainers or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9316" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">business people. To qualify for O </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9330" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa¬†status, the immigrant must demonstrate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9344" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sustained national or international acclaim. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9358" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The U.S. employer must show that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9372" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant will fill a position that requires a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9386" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person of extraordinary ability. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9400" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petitioning employer must also submit a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9414" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">peer review evaluation confirming the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9428" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs international renown and the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9442" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need for such a person. Typically, O status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9456" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">will be granted for the duration of need but </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9470" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no more than three years.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9484" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9498" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">P ‚ÄìPerforming artists, athletes and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9512" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entertainers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9526" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9540" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">P visa status is for performing artists, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9554" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">athletes and entertainers. Immigrants </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9568" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">seeking this category must demonstrate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9582" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial achievement in their field. This </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9596" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status also requires a peer review </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9610" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">evaluation confirming the immigrant‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9624" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">international renown. P-1¬†status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9638" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">principal immigrants; P-2 status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9652" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">essential supporting personnel; P-3 status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9666" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for coaches and trainers; and P-4 status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9680" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for dependents. Generally, P visa status will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9694" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be granted for the duration of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9708" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">engagement or season.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9722" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9736" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employees gaining permanent residence</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9750" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9764" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are two major avenues to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9778" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent¬†residence:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9792" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9806" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">family based sponsorship</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9820" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment-based sponsorship.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9834" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Each type of sponsorship has several </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9848" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">categories and different procedures.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9862" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9876" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrants who marry U.S. citizens may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9890" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sponsored immediately for permanent </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9904" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residence and are not subject to category or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9918" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">per-country quotas. If the sponsor‚Äôs petition </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9932" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is filed within two years after the marriage, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9946" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant will be granted a conditional </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9960" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence and the couple must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9974" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">file a joint petition to remove conditions on </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9988" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residence two years after the immigrant is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10002" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted conditional permanent residence. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10016" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">This requirement is intended to deter </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10030" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">marriage fraud.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10044" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10058" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Almost all other family-based petitions are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10072" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">subject to category and per-country quotas </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10086" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and because of the high level of demand, it </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10100" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">may take many years before a visa is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10114" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available. There are family-based categories </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10128" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for unmarried sons and daughters of U.S. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10142" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">citizens, spouses and children of permanent </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10156" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residents, married sons and daughters of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10170" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. citizens and brothers and sisters of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10184" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. citizens.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10198" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10212" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10226" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">also has several categories. Each has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10240" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">different requirements. For some categories, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10254" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer must obtain ‚Äúlabor </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10268" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certification,‚Äù such as a certification from </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10282" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">DOL that there are no U.S. workers qualified </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10296" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and available to fill the position for which the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10310" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant is sponsored.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10324" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10338" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 1</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10352" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10366" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 1 is for Priority </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10380" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Workers, which includes Nobel laureates, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10394" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">college/university teachers/researchers and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10408" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">intracompany transferee managers/</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10422" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives. Labor certification is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10436" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">required for this category.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10450" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10464" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 2</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10478" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10492" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 2 is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10506" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants with advanced degrees and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10520" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants with exceptional ability in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10534" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">arts, sciences, education, athletics or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10548" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">business. Labor certification is usually </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10562" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">required for this category unless the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10576" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs employment will directly serve </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10590" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">important U.S. interests.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10604" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10618" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 3</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10632" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10646" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 3 is the most </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10660" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">common of the employment-based </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10674" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">categories, as it is used by professionals </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10688" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">without advanced degrees, skilled workers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10702" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in jobs requiring at least two years of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10716" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training or education and unskilled workers. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10730" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Labor certification is always required for this </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10744" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">category.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10758" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10772" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Categories 4 and 5</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10786" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10800" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 4 is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10814" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Religious Workers, but is little-used now </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10828" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">because of a history of abuse. Similarly, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10842" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment-based Category 5, which is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10856" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">investors committing more than $1.8 million </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10870" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the U.S. economy, is also little-used </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10884" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">because of a history of visa fraud.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10898" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10912" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once labor certification is obtained, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10926" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer files a permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10940" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition with CIS. The immigrant and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10954" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependent family members may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10968" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">concurrently file for adjustment of status. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10982" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant has worked without </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10996" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization or failed to maintain lawful </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11010" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status at all times or if a visa is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11024" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately available, the immigrant must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11038" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">complete the permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11052" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure through consular processing at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11066" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. embassy or consulate in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11080" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">native country.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11094" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11108" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The lawful resident verification information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11122" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is the documentation that is required by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11136" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States when completing the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11150" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11164" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11178" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The penalties for employers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11192" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11206" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If an employer knowingly hires, recruits or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11220" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">refers an undocumented immigrant for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11234" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment and a state or local </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11248" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government agency has reason to believe </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11262" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that a violation¬†has occurred, the agency is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11276" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">mandated by law to file a complaint, which </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11290" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">triggers an automatic investigation by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11304" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the commissioner finds </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11318" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11332" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowingly violated the law with respect to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11346" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">hiring, recruiting or referring an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11360" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">undocumented immigrant for employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11374" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the commissioner will conduct a contested </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11388" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">case hearing. If the commissioner </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11402" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">determines that there is clear and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11416" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">convincing evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11430" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">violated the law and the violation occurred </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11444" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">while the employer was acting within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11458" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">parameters of the employer‚Äôs state issued </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11472" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">license, the appropriate regulatory board or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11486" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the local government will revoke, suspend </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11500" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or deny the employer‚Äôs license.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11514" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11528" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If employers do not complete and retain the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11542" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">I-9 form properly, they may face civil money </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11556" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">penalties and possibly criminal penalties as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11570" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">well. Fines for I-9 problems and document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11584" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">abuse discrimination range from $234 to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11598" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$2,332. Penalties for knowingly employing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11612" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">someone who lacks authorization to work </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11626" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">range from $583 to $4,666 for a first </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11640" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense, $4,667 to $11,663 for a second </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11654" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense and $6,999 to $23,333 for a third </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11668" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense. If a person is a federal contractor, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11682" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">they may face debarment for substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11696" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">noncompliance.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11710" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11724" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Following an employer‚Äôs first violation, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11738" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">regulatory board or local government will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11752" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspend the employer‚Äôs license until the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11766" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer shows to the commissioner that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11780" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer is no longer in violation of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11794" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬†law. The employer may make this showing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11808" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a sworn statement with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11822" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the employer commits a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11836" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">second violation within three years of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11850" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">first violation, the employer‚Äôs license will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11864" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspended for one year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11878" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
            </text>

                <tspan x="40" y="120">Welcome to the Federal Human Resources Manual. </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="132">This guide contains details to help you comply with </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="144">federal employment laws. Please note that there are </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="156">also many state laws and ordinances related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="168">managing your employees ‚Äì if you are looking for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="180">complete guide to state and federal laws and </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="192">regulations, visit our resources page to find the what </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="204">is available in your state. Our state-specific Human </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="216">Resources Manuals provide a complete resource for </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="228">all of the employment-related laws affecting your </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="240">business operations.</tspan>

        <g id="chapter-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring-Copy" transform="translate(1680.000000, 0.000000)">
            <g id="Bread-Crumb-&gt;-Title" transform="translate(-1.000000, 56.000000)">
                <g id="Group-4">
                    <g id="Group-2">
                        <rect id="Rectangle" stroke="#FFFFFF" fill="#FFFFFF" x="0.5" y="0.5" width="319" height="46" rx="8"></rect>
                        <text id="1.-Recruiting-and-hi" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="14" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.105000004" fill="#000000">
                            <tspan x="20" y="32">1. Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                        </text>
                    </g>
                    <text id="Federal-Human-Resour" font-family="Helvetica" font-size="6" font-weight="normal" letter-spacing="0.0450000018">
                        <tspan x="20" y="12" fill="#A62424" text-decoration="underline">Federal Human Resources Manual</tspan>
                        <tspan x="114.393945" y="12" fill="#000000"> / </tspan>
                        <tspan x="119.529922" y="12" fill="#AAAAAA">Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                    </text>
                </g>
                <line x1="0.5" y1="46.5" x2="320.5" y2="46.5" id="Line" stroke="#979797" stroke-width="0.5" stroke-linecap="square"></line>
            </g>
            <text id="Text-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="12" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.0900000036" fill="#000000">
                <tspan x="39" y="131">Verification of employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="145" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="159" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Federal law</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="173" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="187" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The Immigration Reform and Control </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="201" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Act¬†(IRCA) requires employers to employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="215" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">only those persons authorized to work in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="229" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this country. Employers are required to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="243" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verify¬†the identity and employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="257" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of all individuals hired after November 6, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="271" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">1986, regardless of how many people the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="285" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company employs. Verification of identity </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="299" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and employment eligibility is accomplished </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="313" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by completing Form I-9. An employer should </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="327" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be careful not to engage in document abuse </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="341" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrimination in this process by specifying </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="355" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">what documents the employee presents, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="369" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requiring more documents than are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="383" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">minimally necessary or rejecting documents </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="397" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that reasonably appear to be genuine.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="411" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="425" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should keep I-9 forms for at least </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="439" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">three years from the date of hire and for one </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="453" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year from the date employment terminates. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="467" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once an employer is certain they have met </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="481" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">both tests, the forms should be thrown </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="495" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">away. An employer is allowed to make </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="509" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies of the documents presented by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="523" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employee, but they must still complete </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="537" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the form also. Under present regulations, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="551" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the retention rules do not apply to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="565" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="579" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="593" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee presents a work </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="607" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document with an expiration </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="621" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">date, the employer must reverify </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="635" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment eligibility before that document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="649" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">expires. Reverification is accomplished by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="663" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">examining a new document and completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="677" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Section 3 of the I-9 form. Employers do not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="691" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need to reverify U.S. passports and I-551 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="705" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Permanent Resident or Resident </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="719" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrant) cards.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="733" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="747" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee cannot present an original </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="761" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document for employment eligibility, an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="775" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer may accept a receipt for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="789" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">replacement employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="803" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document. The receipt will allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="817" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment for 90 days from the date of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="831" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receipt or the date the prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="845" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization expired, whichever is later. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="859" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Remember that the employer will need to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="873" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reverify employment eligibility at the end of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="887" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the 90-day ‚Äúgrace‚Äù period.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="901" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="915" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Note: Employers cannot accept receipts if </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="929" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employment will last three days or less.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="943" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="957" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The government must give three-days‚Äô </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="971" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">notice in writing before inspecting I-9 forms. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="985" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should use this time wisely to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="999" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">ensure that their forms are correctly </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1013" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">completed and that they have all the forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1027" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that should be retained. As a general rule, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1041" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employers should politely insist upon their </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1055" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">right to advance notice of an audit and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1069" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">should not waive their rights by agreeing to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1083" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an inspection of only a handful of forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1097" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1111" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1125">No match letters</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1139" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1153" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">As of September 14, 2007, Immigration and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1167" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Customs Enforcement¬†(ICE) has changed </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1181" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the regulations relating to the unlawful hiring </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1195" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or continued employment of unauthorized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1209" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants. The amended regulations apply </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1223" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the employment verification process and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1237" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">impose new obligations on employers when </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1251" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an employer either:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1265" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1279" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a ‚Äúno match‚Äù letter from the Social </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1293" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Security Administration</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1307" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a letter regarding employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1321" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verification forms from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1335" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1349" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The new regulation has been criticized by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1363" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">some as a back-door way for the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1377" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government to address the nation‚Äôs growing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1391" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal immigration population in the wake of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1405" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">repeated failures by Congress to pass a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1419" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">comprehensive immigration reform bill.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1433" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1447" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the new regulation, employers have a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1461" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">heightened duty to follow up on no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1475" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">letters and other employment verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1489" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancies. The Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1503" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security takes the position that a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1517" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no-match letter is a distinct indication that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1531" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the subject employee is not authorized to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1545" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in the United States. The regulation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1559" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">creates an expansive definition of the term </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1573" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúconstructive knowledge‚Äù as applied to an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1587" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs information about an individual‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1601" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work in the United States </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1615" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the Immigration and Nationality Act.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1629" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1643" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An employer may violate federal regulations </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1657" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">if it has knowledge that an employee is an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1671" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker. An employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1685" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">deemed to have knowledge if a reasonable </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1699" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person would infer from the facts that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1713" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee is unauthorized. Constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1727" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge can be found where one of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1741" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following is true:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1755" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1769" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The I-9 form employment eligibility form has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1783" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not been properly completed (including </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1797" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">support documentation).</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1811" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer has learned that the worker is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1825" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not authorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1839" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1853" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer acts with reckless disregard </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1867" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for the legal consequences or permitting </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1881" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">another individual to introduce an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1895" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker into the workforce.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1909" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Examples of an employer‚Äôs constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1923" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge that an employee may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1937" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work include:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1951" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1965" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Social Security </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1979" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Administration that the combination of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1993" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">name and social security number submitted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2007" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for an employee do not match agency </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2021" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2035" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2049" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security that the immigration </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2063" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status document or employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2077" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document presented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2091" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referenced by the employee in completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2105" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9 was assigned to another person or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2119" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the agency has no record that the document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2133" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has been assigned</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2147" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a request by a worker (who already claimed </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2161" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to be a permanent resident, U.S. citizen or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2175" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. national) that the employer file an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2189" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant labor certification or employment-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2203" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">based immigration visa petition.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2217" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The amended regulation also describes </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2231" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúsafe harbor‚Äù procedures that the employer </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2245" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">can follow in response to such a letter and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2259" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">thereby be certain that the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2273" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security will not use the letter as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2287" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">part of an allegation that the employer had </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2301" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">constructive knowledge that the employee </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2315" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referred to in the letter is an immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2329" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2343" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.¬† The ‚Äúsafe harbor‚Äù procedures </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2357" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">include attempting to resolve the no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2371" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">issue and, if it cannot be resolved within a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2385" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certain period of time, independently </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2399" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verifying the employee‚Äôs identity and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2413" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment authorization through a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2427" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialized process.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2441" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2455" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigration and Customs Enforcement </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2469" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">considers employers to have acted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2483" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reasonably if the employer resolves the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2497" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancy with the relevant agency within </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2511" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">30 days of receiving a no match letter by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2525" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">doing all of the following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2539" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2553" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">checking its records for a clerical error</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2567" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">informing the agency of its error</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2581" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verifying that the name and number, as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2595" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">corrected, match the agency‚Äôs records.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2609" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employer cannot resolve the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2623" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancy as described above, it must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2637" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">contact the employee and request </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2651" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">confirmation that the employee‚Äôs information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2665" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is correct. If the original information was </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2679" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct, the employer must do all of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2693" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2707" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2721" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct the employee‚Äôs information in its </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2735" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2749" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">inform the relevant agency of the correction</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2763" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">match the corrected information with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2777" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">agency‚Äôs records.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2791" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee who is the subject of a no-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2805" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">match letter maintains that the information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2819" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">he or she provided to the employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2833" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct, the employer must ask the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2847" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee to pursue the matter him or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2861" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">herself with the agency. Employers who </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2875" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">take these corrective steps within 30 days of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2889" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receiving a no-match letter are regarded as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2903" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">having acted reasonably and fall within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2917" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">safe-harbor.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2931" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2945" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Likewise, many states have laws making it </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2959" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal for an employer to knowingly employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2973" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or refer for employment any individual who </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2987" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has illegally entered the United States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3001" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3015">Temporary visas</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3029" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3043" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. employers may sponsor foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3057" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employees for certain temporary </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3071" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa¬†categories that authorize employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3085" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in this country. Some of these categories </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3099" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">include:¬†</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3113" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3127" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B ‚Äì Specialty occupation (professional)</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3141" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3155" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B visa is for professionals who will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3169" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in a ‚Äúspecialty occupation‚Äù on a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3183" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary basis for no more than six years. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3197" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The duration of stay is three years, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3211" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">extendable to six years. An exception to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3225" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">maximum length of stay applies in certain </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3239" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">circumstances. A specialty occupation is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3253" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">one that requires:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3267" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3281" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">theoretical and practical application of a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3295" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">body of highly specialized knowledge</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3309" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">attainment of a bachelor‚Äôs or higher degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3323" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in the specific specialty (or its equivalent) as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3337" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a minimum for entry into the occupation in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3351" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3365" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are numerous occupations that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3379" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">potentially qualify as specialty occupations. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3393" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer must prove -- through </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3407" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">objective evidence -- that the job offered </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3421" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">falls within the statutory and regulatory </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3435" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">definitions set forth.¬† Typical occupations </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3449" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualifying for H1B visa status include </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3463" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professions, which are defined by INA </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3477" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬ß101(a)(32) to include architects, engineers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3491" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">lawyers, physicians, surgeons and teachers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3505" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in elementary or secondary schools, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3519" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">colleges, academies or seminaries. H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3533" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visas are employer and job specific.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3547" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3561" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Current laws limit the annual number of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3575" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualifying foreign workers who may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3589" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">issued a visa or otherwise be provided H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3603" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status to 65,000 with an additional 20,000 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3617" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the H-1B advanced degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3631" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">exemption.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3645" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3659" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B1 (Chile and Singapore) program </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3673" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">allows employers to temporarily employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3687" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign workers from Chile and Singapore in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3701" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States on a nonimmigrant basis </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3715" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in specialty occupations. Current laws limit </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3729" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the annual number of qualifying foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3743" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">workers who may be issued an H-1B1 visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3757" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to 6,800 with 1,400 from Chile and 5,400 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3771" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">from Singapore.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3785" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3799" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B petition process involves </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3813" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certification of a labor condition </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3827" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">application¬†(LCA) by the U.S. Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3841" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Labor (DOL) and approval of an H-1B visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3855" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition filed with the USCIS. Employers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3869" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must submit an LCA to the DOL </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3883" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">electronically through the FLAG system </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3897" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">attesting to compliance with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3911" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirements of H-1B or H-1B1. LCAs must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3925" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not be submitted more than six months </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3939" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before the beginning date of the period of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3953" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment. The two exceptions to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3967" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">electronic filing are employers with physical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3981" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">disabilities or those who lack Internet </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="3995" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">access and cannot electronically file the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4009" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form ETA-9035E. An employer must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4023" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition the administrator of OFLC for prior </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4037" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">special permission to file an LCA by mail on </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4051" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the Form ETA-9035.¬† After the employer‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4065" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B petition is approved by USCIS, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4079" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">individual worker can obtain an H-1B visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4093" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">stamp by appointment at the U.S. consulate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4107" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or embassy in his or her native country. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4121" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the individual is already in the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4135" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States, a change of status to H-1B is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4149" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">possible; and if the individual is already in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4163" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B status, he or she can begin working </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4177" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for a new H-1B employer as soon as the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4191" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs petition is filed without having to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4205" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">wait for an approval. The LCA verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4219" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">process requires the employer to certify that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4233" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4247" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4261" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B individual will be paid the higher of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4275" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">prevailing or actual wage for that occupation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4289" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in the area of intended employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4303" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will offer the individual the same </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4317" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">terms and conditions of employment that it </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4331" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offers to U.S. workers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4345" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment of the noncitizen will not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4359" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">adversely affect the wages and working </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4373" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">conditions of workers similarly employed in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4387" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the area of intended employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4401" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will not employ the individual in a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4415" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">strike or lockout or work stoppage related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4429" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a labor dispute in the occupation at the time </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4443" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the application is signed</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4457" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will notify other similarly situated </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4471" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employees (or their agent) of its intent to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4485" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employ an H-1B individual in the relevant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4499" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">position.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4513" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer must also document its </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4527" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">compliance with the LCA verifications by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4541" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">retaining relevant documents and by making </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4555" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available a ‚Äúpublic inspection‚Äù file upon </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4569" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">request.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4583" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4597" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B status is initially granted for no more </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4611" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">than three years. Extensions are available, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4625" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">but the employee is subject to a maximum </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4639" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">cumulative period of six years of H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4653" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status. H-1B extensions beyond the six-year </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4667" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">limit are possible if the individual is the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4681" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">beneficiary of an employment-based </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4695" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence process that has been </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4709" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">pending for more than one year or is the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4723" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">beneficiary of an approved immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4737" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition and is unable to adjust status to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4751" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence because of per-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4765" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country limits.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4779" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4793" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer will be liable for the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4807" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reasonable costs of the foreign national's </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4821" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">return transportation if the employer </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4835" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">terminates the foreign national before the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4849" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">end of the foreign national's period of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4863" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorized stay. The employer is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4877" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">responsible for the costs of foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4891" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">national's return transportation if foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4905" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">national voluntarily resigns the position.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4919" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4933" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Treaty NAFTA ‚Äì Canadian and Mexican </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4947" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professionals</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4961" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4975" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the North American Free Trade </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="4989" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Agreement¬†(NAFTA), citizens of Canada </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5003" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and Mexico who are qualified professionals </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5017" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">can work in the United States using the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5031" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Treaty NAFTA or TN, classification. This </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5045" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa category is available for designated </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5059" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professional occupations set forth in an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5073" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">appendix to NAFTA. The list of professions </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5087" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">includes many occupations that would also </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5101" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualify for H-1 status, such as engineers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5115" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">accountants and professors. One advantage </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5129" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of TN status is that the application </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5143" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure is very simple. An applicant can </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5157" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">apply at the border by presenting all of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5171" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5185" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5199" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">proof of Canadian or Mexican citizenship</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5213" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">proof of membership in a listed occupation</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5227" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an offer of employment in that occupation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5241" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">from a U.S. employer</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5255" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$50.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5269" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The ‚Äúapplication‚Äù is adjudicated on-the-spot </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5283" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and, if approved, the immigrant is given a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5297" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">multiple-entry TN status good for one year.¬†¬†</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5311" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5325" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Although TN status can theoretically be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5339" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">renewed indefinitely in one-year increments </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5353" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a petition or by reapplying at the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5367" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">border, in practice the status may be limited </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5381" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to five or six years of renewals because the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5395" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">treaty states that TN status cannot be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5409" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted to an immigrant who intends to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5423" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reside in the United States permanently. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5437" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of TN immigrants can get TD </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5451" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Treaty Dependent) status but cannot use </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5465" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that status to work in this country.</tspan>
