                <tspan x="39" y="5479" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5493" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1A and L-1B ‚Äì Intracompany transfers of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5507" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managers/executives or specialized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5521" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge personnel</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5535" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5549" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The L-1A¬†and L-1B visas are designed to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5563" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">facilitate the temporary transfer of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5577" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managerial, executive and specialized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5591" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge personnel from overseas entities </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5605" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to related U.S. entities. L-1A status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5619" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managers and executives and L-1B status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5633" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for persons with specialized knowledge of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5647" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company methods, products, procedures, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5661" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">operations, etc. To qualify for L-1 status, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5675" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee must have worked for the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5689" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company abroad in a managerial, executive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5703" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or specialized knowledge position for at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5717" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">least one full year during the three years </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5731" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">prior to the transfer to a managerial, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5745" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executive or specialized knowledge position </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5759" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">with the related U.S. entity. First line </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5773" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">supervisors are not eligible for L-1A status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5787" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">as managers unless the persons they </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5801" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">supervise are professionals.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5815" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5829" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The U.S. employer must file a petition for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5843" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1 status with the regional USCIS Service </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5857" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Center with jurisdiction over the location </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5871" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">where the immigrant will work. Canadian </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5885" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferees may submit the petition at the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5899" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S.-Canada border for immediate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5913" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">adjudication. Once the employer‚Äôs petition is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5927" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">approved, the immigrant may obtain an L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5941" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa stamp from the U.S. embassy or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5955" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">consulate abroad or if already in the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5969" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States, may commence the L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5983" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="5997" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6011" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1 status is initially granted for three years </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6025" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and extensions are available for two-year </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6039" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">periods. L-1A managers/executives are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6053" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entitled to up to seven years of L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6067" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment in the United States and L-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6081" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialized knowledge personnel are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6095" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">eligible for a maximum of five years of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6109" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorized stay. Dependents of L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6123" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferees obtain L-2 status. Unlike most </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6137" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary visa categories that do not allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6151" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependents to work, L-2 spouses may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6165" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">obtain employment authorization.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6179" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6193" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Some multi-national companies may qualify </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6207" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for ‚Äúblanket‚Äù L-1 status. Typically, this is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6221" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available for entities that transfer more than </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6235" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">10 people per year, have annual sales in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6249" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">excess of $25 million or more than 1,000 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6263" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. employees. Blanket L-1 status allows </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6277" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. entity to bypass the USCIS petition </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6291" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">process in individual cases. Instead, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6305" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. entity sends a special form to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6319" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferee, who then applies for L-1 status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6333" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">directly at the U.S. consulate or embassy.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6347" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6361" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1 and E-2 ‚Äì Treaty trader/investor</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6375" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6389" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Based upon a bilateral investment treaty or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6403" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a treaty of friendship, navigation and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6417" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commerce between the United States and a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6431" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign country, an individual may come to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6445" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States to open and operate a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6459" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign-owned business or be employed in a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6473" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign-owned business that already exists </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6487" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">here. Entities engaged in substantial trade </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6501" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">between the United States and the treaty </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6515" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country will be able to transfer managers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6529" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives and key personnel using the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6543" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1¬†(Treaty Trader) visa status. Entities </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6557" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">making a substantial investment in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6571" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States may transfer managers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6585" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives and key personnel using the E-2 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6599" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Treaty Investor) visa status.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6613" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6627" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The foreign entity must be a ‚Äúcitizen‚Äù or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6641" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúnative‚Äù of the treaty country. This means </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6655" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that at least a majority of the ownership of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6669" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the foreign entity must be held by citizens of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6683" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the treaty country. The person seeking E </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6697" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa status must also be a citizen of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6711" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">treaty country. There is no prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6725" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirement, however.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6739" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6753" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1 immigrants must be engaged in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6767" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">activities supporting a substantial volume of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6781" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">international trade in goods or services. E-2 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6795" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants must be directing or developing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6809" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an active and substantial investment of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6823" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">irrevocably committed funds devoted to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6837" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">production of goods or services. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6851" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚ÄúSubstantial‚Äù means more than enough to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6865" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">secure the success of the enterprise and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6879" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">more than enough to support the E </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6893" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant and family members.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6907" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6921" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Most E immigrants apply for E visa status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6935" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">directly at the U.S. embassy or consulate in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6949" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the treaty country, but it is possible to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6963" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">change to E status from within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6977" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States Immigrants admitted in E status are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="6991" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted two years of authorized stay so long </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7005" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">as their E visa stamp is valid at the time of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7019" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entry. Typically, E visas are valid for five </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7033" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">years, but this may vary depending upon </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7047" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the terms of the treaty. In most cases, the E </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7061" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa can be renewed for additional periods </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7075" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">provided that the underlying trade or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7089" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">investment remains viable.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7103" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7117" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of E visa immigrants acquire </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7131" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the same status as the principal immigrant, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7145" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">such as E-1 or E-2 status. E-2 spouses may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7159" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">obtain employment authorization.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7173" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7187" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2A and H-2B ‚Äì Agricultural and other </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7201" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">seasonal and temporary workers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7215" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7229" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-2A visa¬†is for seasonal agricultural </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7243" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">workers and the H-2B visa¬†is for non-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7257" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">agricultural temporary or seasonal workers. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7271" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2 status is only available for jobs that are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7285" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">truly temporary in nature, so the status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7299" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">almost always limited to one year. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7313" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer must test the market for available </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7327" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. workers and obtain a certification from </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7341" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">DOL that none are available to fill the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7355" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary position(s). The test of the market </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7369" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must offer prevailing wages and working </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7383" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">conditions.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7397" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7411" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There is a quota or limit on the number of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7425" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2B visas that can be issued each fiscal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7439" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year. Often, the quota is exhausted well </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7453" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before the end of the fiscal year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7467" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7481" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2A employers may be required to hire </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7495" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. workers who apply for work anytime up </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7509" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to halfway through the certification period, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7523" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">even if that involves discharging the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7537" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant worker. Also, H-2A employers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7551" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">may need to pay special wages, offer </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7565" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">housing and in some cases may have to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7579" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">pay transportation costs for the immigrant to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7593" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">come to the work site and return home.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7607" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7621" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Each H-2 period of authorized stay will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7635" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">one year or less. After using three </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7649" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">consecutive H-2 periods, the immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7663" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must remain outside the United States for at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7677" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">least six months before becoming eligible to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7691" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">use H-2 status again.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7705" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7719" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-3 ‚ÄìTrainees</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7733" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7747" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">A U.S. employer may sponsor an immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7761" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for H-3¬†status to provide the immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7775" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training that is unavailable in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7789" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs native country. The immigrant is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7803" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not supposed to engage in productive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7817" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training other than as necessary to provide </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7831" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">effective training. H-3 immigrants cannot </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7845" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">displace U.S. workers. The petitioning </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7859" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer must supply extensive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7873" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">documentation of an appropriate training </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7887" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">curriculum with the petition. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7901" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">documentation must specifically discuss the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7915" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">amount of on-the-job vs. classroom training, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7929" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">address why the training is not available in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7943" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the trainee‚Äôs native country and explain how </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7957" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the training experience will enhance the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7971" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs career prospects abroad. H-3 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7985" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status is limited to the duration of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="7999" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training program, which cannot exceed two </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8013" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">years.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8027" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8041" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-1 ‚ÄìAcademic students</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8055" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8069" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-l visas¬†are for students engaged in degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8083" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">programs at U.S. academic institutions. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8097" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are several types of employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8111" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization available to F-l foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8125" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">students, including on-campus employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8139" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">off-campus employment due to severe </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8153" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">economic hardship, international </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8167" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">organization internships, curricular practical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8181" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training and optional practical training </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8195" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before and after completion of studies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8209" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8223" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An F-l student engaged in a full course of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8237" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">study may engage in part-time on-campus </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8251" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment such as working in a cafeteria </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8265" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or bookstore so long as this employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8279" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">does not displace a U.S. worker. This type </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8293" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of on-campus employment does not require </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8307" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">advance permission from USCIS.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8321" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8335" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An F-l student may apply for employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8349" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work off-campus due to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8363" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">economic necessity or for an internship with </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8377" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an international organization. Economic </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8391" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">necessity work permits are normally not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8405" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted except upon proof of a substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8419" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and unforeseen change in the student‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8433" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">finances.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8447" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8461" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-1 students may also engage in practical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8475" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training employment related to their degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8489" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">program. While enrolled, F-1 students may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8503" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">use Curricular Practical Training. This may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8517" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">take the form of an internship, co-op, work-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8531" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">study program or some other activity that is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8545" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an integral part of the degree program and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8559" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">CPT can be commenced upon an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8573" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">endorsement by the school‚Äôs foreign student </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8587" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">advisor. A student who uses more than 12 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8601" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">months of CPT becomes ineligible for post-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8615" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">graduate Optional Practical Training¬†(OPT).</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8629" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8643" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">OPT permits up to 12 months of on-the-job </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8657" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">practical training upon completion of an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8671" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">academic degree program. F-1 students </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8685" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must apply for a work permit in order to use </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8699" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">OPT and cannot commence employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8713" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">until the permit is issued.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8727" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8741" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of F-1 immigrants are granted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8755" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-2 status and cannot work.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8769" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8783" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">J-1 ‚ÄìExchange visitors</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8797" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8811" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrants participating in a designated </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8825" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">exchange visitor program may engage in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8839" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specific types of employment as part of their </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8853" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">program activities. There are many types of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8867" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">J-1 exchange visitor programs, including </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8881" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">those for students, practical trainees, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8895" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">teachers, professors, research assistants, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8909" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialists, camp counselors, au pairs and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8923" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">distinguished visitors. J-1 practical trainees </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8937" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">are authorized up to 18 months of on-the-</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8951" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">job training; other categories have different </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8965" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">time limits.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8979" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="8993" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Some exchange visitors are subject to a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9007" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">two-year home country residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9021" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirement that must be satisfied before </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9035" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant is eligible for H, L or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9049" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent resident status. This obligation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9063" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">arises if the immigrant‚Äôs exchange visit is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9077" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">funded by the immigrant‚Äôs government or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9091" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. government, if the immigrant‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9105" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">skills are in short supply in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9119" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country or if the immigrant is coming to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9133" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States to obtain graduate medical </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9147" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">education. If the immigrant is subject to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9161" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">two-year residence requirement, so too are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9175" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">all of the immigrant‚Äôs dependents. It is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9189" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sometimes possible to obtain a waiver of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9203" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this requirement, but the waiver process is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9217" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">cumbersome and time-consuming.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9231" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9245" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">O ‚ÄìExtraordinary ability immigrants</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9259" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9273" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The O category is for highly talented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9287" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">acclaimed individuals who are scientists, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9301" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">educators, artists, athletes, entertainers or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9315" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">business people. To qualify for O </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9329" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa¬†status, the immigrant must demonstrate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9343" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sustained national or international acclaim. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9357" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The U.S. employer must show that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9371" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant will fill a position that requires a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9385" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person of extraordinary ability. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9399" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petitioning employer must also submit a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9413" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">peer review evaluation confirming the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9427" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs international renown and the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9441" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need for such a person. Typically, O status </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9455" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">will be granted for the duration of need but </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9469" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no more than three years.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9483" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9497" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">P ‚ÄìPerforming artists, athletes and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9511" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entertainers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9525" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9539" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">P visa status is for performing artists, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9553" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">athletes and entertainers. Immigrants </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9567" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">seeking this category must demonstrate </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9581" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial achievement in their field. This </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9595" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status also requires a peer review </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9609" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">evaluation confirming the immigrant‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9623" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">international renown. P-1¬†status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9637" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">principal immigrants; P-2 status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9651" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">essential supporting personnel; P-3 status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9665" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for coaches and trainers; and P-4 status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9679" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for dependents. Generally, P visa status will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9693" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be granted for the duration of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9707" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">engagement or season.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9721" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9735" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employees gaining permanent residence</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9749" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9763" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are two major avenues to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9777" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent¬†residence:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9791" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9805" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">family based sponsorship</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9819" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment-based sponsorship.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9833" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Each type of sponsorship has several </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9847" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">categories and different procedures.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9861" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9875" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrants who marry U.S. citizens may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9889" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sponsored immediately for permanent </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9903" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residence and are not subject to category or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9917" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">per-country quotas. If the sponsor‚Äôs petition </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9931" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is filed within two years after the marriage, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9945" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant will be granted a conditional </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9959" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence and the couple must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9973" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">file a joint petition to remove conditions on </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="9987" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residence two years after the immigrant is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10001" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted conditional permanent residence. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10015" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">This requirement is intended to deter </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10029" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">marriage fraud.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10043" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10057" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Almost all other family-based petitions are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10071" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">subject to category and per-country quotas </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10085" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and because of the high level of demand, it </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10099" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">may take many years before a visa is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10113" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available. There are family-based categories </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10127" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for unmarried sons and daughters of U.S. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10141" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">citizens, spouses and children of permanent </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10155" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residents, married sons and daughters of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10169" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. citizens and brothers and sisters of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10183" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. citizens.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10197" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10211" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10225" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">also has several categories. Each has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10239" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">different requirements. For some categories, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10253" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer must obtain ‚Äúlabor </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10267" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certification,‚Äù such as a certification from </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10281" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">DOL that there are no U.S. workers qualified </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10295" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and available to fill the position for which the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10309" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant is sponsored.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10323" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10337" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 1</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10351" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10365" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 1 is for Priority </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10379" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Workers, which includes Nobel laureates, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10393" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">college/university teachers/researchers and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10407" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">intracompany transferee managers/</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10421" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives. Labor certification is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10435" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">required for this category.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10449" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10463" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 2</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10477" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10491" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 2 is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10505" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants with advanced degrees and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10519" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants with exceptional ability in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10533" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">arts, sciences, education, athletics or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10547" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">business. Labor certification is usually </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10561" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">required for this category unless the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10575" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs employment will directly serve </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10589" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">important U.S. interests.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10603" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10617" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 3</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10631" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10645" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 3 is the most </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10659" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">common of the employment-based </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10673" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">categories, as it is used by professionals </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10687" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">without advanced degrees, skilled workers </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10701" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in jobs requiring at least two years of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10715" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training or education and unskilled workers. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10729" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Labor certification is always required for this </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10743" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">category.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10757" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10771" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Categories 4 and 5</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10785" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10799" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 4 is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10813" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Religious Workers, but is little-used now </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10827" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">because of a history of abuse. Similarly, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10841" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment-based Category 5, which is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10855" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">investors committing more than $1.8 million </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10869" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the U.S. economy, is also little-used </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10883" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">because of a history of visa fraud.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10897" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10911" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once labor certification is obtained, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10925" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer files a permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10939" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition with CIS. The immigrant and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10953" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependent family members may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10967" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">concurrently file for adjustment of status. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10981" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant has worked without </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10995" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization or failed to maintain lawful </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11009" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status at all times or if a visa is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11023" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately available, the immigrant must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11037" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">complete the permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11051" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure through consular processing at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11065" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. embassy or consulate in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11079" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">native country.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11093" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11107" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The lawful resident verification information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11121" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is the documentation that is required by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11135" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States when completing the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11149" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11163" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11177" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The penalties for employers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11191" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11205" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If an employer knowingly hires, recruits or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11219" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">refers an undocumented immigrant for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11233" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment and a state or local </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11247" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government agency has reason to believe </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11261" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that a violation¬†has occurred, the agency is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11275" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">mandated by law to file a complaint, which </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11289" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">triggers an automatic investigation by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11303" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the commissioner finds </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11317" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11331" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowingly violated the law with respect to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11345" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">hiring, recruiting or referring an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11359" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">undocumented immigrant for employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11373" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the commissioner will conduct a contested </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11387" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">case hearing. If the commissioner </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11401" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">determines that there is clear and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11415" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">convincing evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11429" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">violated the law and the violation occurred </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11443" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">while the employer was acting within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11457" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">parameters of the employer‚Äôs state issued </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11471" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">license, the appropriate regulatory board or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11485" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the local government will revoke, suspend </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11499" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or deny the employer‚Äôs license.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11513" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11527" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If employers do not complete and retain the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11541" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">I-9 form properly, they may face civil money </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11555" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">penalties and possibly criminal penalties as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11569" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">well. Fines for I-9 problems and document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11583" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">abuse discrimination range from $234 to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11597" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$2,332. Penalties for knowingly employing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11611" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">someone who lacks authorization to work </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11625" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">range from $583 to $4,666 for a first </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11639" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense, $4,667 to $11,663 for a second </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11653" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense and $6,999 to $23,333 for a third </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11667" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense. If a person is a federal contractor, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11681" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">they may face debarment for substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11695" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">noncompliance.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11709" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11723" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Following an employer‚Äôs first violation, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11737" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">regulatory board or local government will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11751" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspend the employer‚Äôs license until the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11765" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer shows to the commissioner that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11779" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer is no longer in violation of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11793" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬†law. The employer may make this showing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11807" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a sworn statement with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11821" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the employer commits a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11835" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">second violation within three years of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11849" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">first violation, the employer‚Äôs license will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11863" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspended for one year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11877" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
            </text>

                <tspan x="40" y="132">This guide contains details to help you comply with </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="144">federal employment laws. Please note that there are </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="156">also many state laws and ordinances related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="168">managing your employees ‚Äì if you are looking for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="180">complete guide to state and federal laws and </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="192">regulations, visit our resources page to find the what </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="204">is available in your state. Our state-specific Human </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="216">Resources Manuals provide a complete resource for </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="228">all of the employment-related laws affecting your </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="240">business operations.</tspan>
            </text>

        <g id="chapter-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring-Copy-3" transform="translate(3360.000000, 0.000000)">
            <g id="Bread-Crumb-&gt;-Title" transform="translate(-1.000000, 56.000000)">
                <g id="Group-4">
                    <g id="Group-2">
                        <rect id="Rectangle" stroke="#FFFFFF" fill="#FFFFFF" x="0.5" y="0.5" width="319" height="46" rx="8"></rect>
                        <text id="1.-Recruiting-and-hi" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="14" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.105000004" fill="#000000">
                            <tspan x="20" y="32">1. Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                        </text>
                    </g>
                    <text id="Federal-Human-Resour" font-family="Helvetica" font-size="6" font-weight="normal" letter-spacing="0.0450000018">
                        <tspan x="20" y="12" fill="#24A649" text-decoration="underline">Federal Human Resources Manual</tspan>
                        <tspan x="114.393945" y="12" fill="#000000"> / </tspan>
                        <tspan x="119.529922" y="12" fill="#AAAAAA">Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                    </text>
                </g>
                <line x1="0.5" y1="46.5" x2="320.5" y2="46.5" id="Line" stroke="#979797" stroke-width="0.5" stroke-linecap="square"></line>
            </g>
            <text id="Text-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="12" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.0900000036" fill="#000000">
                <tspan x="39" y="131">Verification of employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="145" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="159" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Federal law</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="173" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="187" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The Immigration Reform and Control </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="201" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Act¬†(IRCA) requires employers to employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="215" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">only those persons authorized to work in </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="229" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this country. Employers are required to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="243" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verify¬†the identity and employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="257" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of all individuals hired after November 6, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="271" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">1986, regardless of how many people the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="285" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company employs. Verification of identity </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="299" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and employment eligibility is accomplished </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="313" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by completing Form I-9. An employer should </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="327" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be careful not to engage in document abuse </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="341" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrimination in this process by specifying </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="355" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">what documents the employee presents, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="369" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requiring more documents than are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="383" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">minimally necessary or rejecting documents </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="397" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that reasonably appear to be genuine.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="411" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="425" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should keep I-9 forms for at least </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="439" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">three years from the date of hire and for one </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="453" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year from the date employment terminates. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="467" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once an employer is certain they have met </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="481" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">both tests, the forms should be thrown </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="495" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">away. An employer is allowed to make </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="509" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies of the documents presented by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="523" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employee, but they must still complete </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="537" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the form also. Under present regulations, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="551" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the retention rules do not apply to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="565" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="579" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="593" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee presents a work </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="607" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document with an expiration </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="621" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">date, the employer must reverify </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="635" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment eligibility before that document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="649" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">expires. Reverification is accomplished by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="663" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">examining a new document and completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="677" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Section 3 of the I-9 form. Employers do not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="691" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need to reverify U.S. passports and I-551 </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="705" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Permanent Resident or Resident </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="719" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrant) cards.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="733" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="747" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee cannot present an original </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="761" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document for employment eligibility, an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="775" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer may accept a receipt for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="789" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">replacement employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="803" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document. The receipt will allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="817" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment for 90 days from the date of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="831" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receipt or the date the prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="845" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization expired, whichever is later. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="859" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Remember that the employer will need to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="873" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reverify employment eligibility at the end of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="887" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the 90-day ‚Äúgrace‚Äù period.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="901" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="915" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Note: Employers cannot accept receipts if </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="929" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employment will last three days or less.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="943" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="957" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The government must give three-days‚Äô </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="971" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">notice in writing before inspecting I-9 forms. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="985" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should use this time wisely to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="999" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">ensure that their forms are correctly </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1013" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">completed and that they have all the forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1027" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that should be retained. As a general rule, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1041" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employers should politely insist upon their </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1055" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">right to advance notice of an audit and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1069" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">should not waive their rights by agreeing to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1083" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an inspection of only a handful of forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1097" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1111" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1125">No match letters</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1139" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1153" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">As of September 14, 2007, Immigration and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1167" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Customs Enforcement¬†(ICE) has changed </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1181" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the regulations relating to the unlawful hiring </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1195" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or continued employment of unauthorized </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1209" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants. The amended regulations apply </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1223" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the employment verification process and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1237" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">impose new obligations on employers when </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1251" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an employer either:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1265" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1279" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a ‚Äúno match‚Äù letter from the Social </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1293" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Security Administration</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1307" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a letter regarding employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1321" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verification forms from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1335" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1349" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The new regulation has been criticized by </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1363" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">some as a back-door way for the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1377" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government to address the nation‚Äôs growing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1391" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal immigration population in the wake of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1405" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">repeated failures by Congress to pass a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1419" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">comprehensive immigration reform bill.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1433" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1447" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the new regulation, employers have a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1461" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">heightened duty to follow up on no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1475" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">letters and other employment verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1489" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancies. The Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1503" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security takes the position that a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1517" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no-match letter is a distinct indication that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1531" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the subject employee is not authorized to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1545" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in the United States. The regulation </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1559" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">creates an expansive definition of the term </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1573" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúconstructive knowledge‚Äù as applied to an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1587" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs information about an individual‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1601" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work in the United States </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1615" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the Immigration and Nationality Act.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1629" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1643" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An employer may violate federal regulations </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1657" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">if it has knowledge that an employee is an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1671" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker. An employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1685" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">deemed to have knowledge if a reasonable </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1699" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person would infer from the facts that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1713" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee is unauthorized. Constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1727" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge can be found where one of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1741" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following is true:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1755" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1769" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The I-9 form employment eligibility form has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1783" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not been properly completed (including </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1797" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">support documentation).</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1811" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer has learned that the worker is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1825" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not authorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1839" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1853" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer acts with reckless disregard </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1867" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for the legal consequences or permitting </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1881" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">another individual to introduce an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1895" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker into the workforce.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1909" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Examples of an employer‚Äôs constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1923" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge that an employee may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1937" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work include:</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1951" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1965" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Social Security </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1979" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Administration that the combination of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="1993" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">name and social security number submitted </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2007" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for an employee do not match agency </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2021" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2035" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2049" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security that the immigration </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2063" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status document or employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2077" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document presented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2091" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referenced by the employee in completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2105" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9 was assigned to another person or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2119" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the agency has no record that the document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2133" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has been assigned</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2147" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a request by a worker (who already claimed </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2161" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to be a permanent resident, U.S. citizen or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2175" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. national) that the employer file an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="2189" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant labor certification or employment-</tspan>
