                <tspan x="39" y="10953" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependent family members may </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10967" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">concurrently file for adjustment of status. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10981" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant has worked without </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="10995" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization or failed to maintain lawful </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11009" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status at all times or if a visa is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11023" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately available, the immigrant must </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11037" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">complete the permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11051" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure through consular processing at </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11065" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. embassy or consulate in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11079" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">native country.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11093" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11107" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The lawful resident verification information </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11121" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is the documentation that is required by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11135" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States when completing the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11149" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11163" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11177" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The penalties for employers</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11191" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11205" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If an employer knowingly hires, recruits or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11219" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">refers an undocumented immigrant for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11233" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment and a state or local </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11247" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government agency has reason to believe </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11261" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that a violation¬†has occurred, the agency is </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11275" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">mandated by law to file a complaint, which </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11289" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">triggers an automatic investigation by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11303" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the commissioner finds </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11317" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11331" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowingly violated the law with respect to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11345" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">hiring, recruiting or referring an </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11359" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">undocumented immigrant for employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11373" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the commissioner will conduct a contested </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11387" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">case hearing. If the commissioner </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11401" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">determines that there is clear and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11415" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">convincing evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11429" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">violated the law and the violation occurred </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11443" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">while the employer was acting within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11457" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">parameters of the employer‚Äôs state issued </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11471" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">license, the appropriate regulatory board or </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11485" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the local government will revoke, suspend </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11499" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or deny the employer‚Äôs license.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11513" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11527" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If employers do not complete and retain the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11541" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">I-9 form properly, they may face civil money </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11555" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">penalties and possibly criminal penalties as </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11569" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">well. Fines for I-9 problems and document </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11583" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">abuse discrimination range from $234 to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11597" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$2,332. Penalties for knowingly employing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11611" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">someone who lacks authorization to work </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11625" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">range from $583 to $4,666 for a first </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11639" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense, $4,667 to $11,663 for a second </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11653" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense and $6,999 to $23,333 for a third </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11667" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense. If a person is a federal contractor, </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11681" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">they may face debarment for substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11695" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">noncompliance.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11709" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11723" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Following an employer‚Äôs first violation, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11737" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">regulatory board or local government will </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11751" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspend the employer‚Äôs license until the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11765" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer shows to the commissioner that </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11779" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer is no longer in violation of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11793" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬†law. The employer may make this showing </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11807" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a sworn statement with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11821" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the employer commits a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11835" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">second violation within three years of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11849" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">first violation, the employer‚Äôs license will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11863" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspended for one year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="11877" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
            </text>

            <text id="Welcome-to-the-Feder" font-family="Helvetica" font-size="10" font-weight="normal" letter-spacing="0.075000003" fill="#000000">
                <tspan x="40" y="120">Welcome to the Federal Human Resources Manual. </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="132">This guide contains details to help you comply with </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="144">federal employment laws. Please note that there are </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="156">also many state laws and ordinances related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="168">managing your employees ‚Äì if you are looking for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="180">complete guide to state and federal laws and </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="192">regulations, visit our resources page to find the what </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="204">is available in your state. Our state-specific Human </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="216">Resources Manuals provide a complete resource for </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="228">all of the employment-related laws affecting your </tspan>
                <tspan x="40" y="240">business operations.</tspan>
            </text>

            <rect fill="#000000" x="0" y="0" width="320" height="12055"></rect>
            <g id="Bread-Crumb-&gt;-Title" transform="translate(-1.000000, 57.000000)">
                <g id="Group-4" transform="translate(4.000000, -0.000000)">
                    <g id="Group-2">
                        <rect id="Rectangle" stroke="#000000" fill="#000000" x="0.5" y="0.5" width="316" height="48" rx="8"></rect>
                        <text id="1.-Recruiting-and-hi" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="14" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.105000004" fill="#FFFFFF">
                            <tspan x="19.8125" y="33.1276596">1. Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                        </text>
                    </g>
                    <text id="Federal-Human-Resour" font-family="Helvetica" font-size="6" font-weight="normal" letter-spacing="0.0450000018">
                        <tspan x="15.85" y="12.4042553" fill="#ECAAAA" text-decoration="underline">Federal Human Resources Manual</tspan>
                        <tspan x="110.243945" y="12.4042553" fill="#000000"> / </tspan>
                        <tspan x="115.379922" y="12.4042553" fill="#AAAAAA">Recruiting and hiring</tspan>
                    </text>
                </g>
                <line x1="0.495327103" y1="48.5" x2="317.504673" y2="48.5" id="Line" stroke="#979797" stroke-width="0.5" stroke-linecap="square"></line>
            </g>
            <text id="Text-&gt;-Recruiting-and-hiring" font-family="Helvetica-Bold, Helvetica" font-size="12" font-weight="bold" letter-spacing="0.0900000036" fill="#FFFFFF">
                <tspan x="36" y="144">Verification of employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="158" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="172" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Federal law</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="186" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="200" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The Immigration Reform and Control </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="214" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Act¬†(IRCA) requires employers to employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="228" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">only those persons authorized to work in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="242" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this country. Employers are required to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="256" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verify¬†the identity and employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="270" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of all individuals hired after November 6, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="284" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">1986, regardless of how many people the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="298" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company employs. Verification of identity </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="312" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and employment eligibility is accomplished </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="326" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by completing Form I-9. An employer should </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="340" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be careful not to engage in document abuse </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="354" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrimination in this process by specifying </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="368" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">what documents the employee presents, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="382" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requiring more documents than are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="396" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">minimally necessary or rejecting documents </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="410" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that reasonably appear to be genuine.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="424" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="438" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should keep I-9 forms for at least </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="452" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">three years from the date of hire and for one </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="466" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year from the date employment terminates. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="480" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once an employer is certain they have met </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="494" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">both tests, the forms should be thrown </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="508" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">away. An employer is allowed to make </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="522" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies of the documents presented by </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="536" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employee, but they must still complete </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="550" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the form also. Under present regulations, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="564" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the retention rules do not apply to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="578" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">photocopies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="592" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="606" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee presents a work </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="620" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document with an expiration </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="634" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">date, the employer must reverify </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="648" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment eligibility before that document </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="662" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">expires. Reverification is accomplished by </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="676" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">examining a new document and completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="690" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Section 3 of the I-9 form. Employers do not </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="704" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need to reverify U.S. passports and I-551 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="718" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Permanent Resident or Resident </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="732" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrant) cards.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="746" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="760" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee cannot present an original </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="774" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document for employment eligibility, an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="788" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer may accept a receipt for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="802" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">replacement employment eligibility </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="816" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">document. The receipt will allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="830" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment for 90 days from the date of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="844" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receipt or the date the prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="858" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization expired, whichever is later. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="872" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Remember that the employer will need to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="886" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reverify employment eligibility at the end of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="900" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the 90-day ‚Äúgrace‚Äù period.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="914" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="928" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Note: Employers cannot accept receipts if </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="942" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employment will last three days or less.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="956" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="970" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The government must give three-days‚Äô </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="984" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">notice in writing before inspecting I-9 forms. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="998" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employers should use this time wisely to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1012" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">ensure that their forms are correctly </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1026" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">completed and that they have all the forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1040" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that should be retained. As a general rule, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1054" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employers should politely insist upon their </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1068" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">right to advance notice of an audit and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1082" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">should not waive their rights by agreeing to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1096" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an inspection of only a handful of forms </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1110" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1124" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1138">No match letters</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1152" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1166" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">As of September 14, 2007, Immigration and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1180" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Customs Enforcement¬†(ICE) has changed </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1194" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the regulations relating to the unlawful hiring </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1208" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or continued employment of unauthorized </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1222" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants. The amended regulations apply </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1236" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the employment verification process and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1250" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">impose new obligations on employers when </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1264" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an employer either:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1278" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1292" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a ‚Äúno match‚Äù letter from the Social </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1306" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Security Administration</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1320" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receives a letter regarding employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1334" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verification forms from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1348" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1362" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The new regulation has been criticized by </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1376" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">some as a back-door way for the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1390" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government to address the nation‚Äôs growing </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1404" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal immigration population in the wake of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1418" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">repeated failures by Congress to pass a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1432" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">comprehensive immigration reform bill.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1446" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1460" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the new regulation, employers have a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1474" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">heightened duty to follow up on no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1488" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">letters and other employment verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1502" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancies. The Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1516" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security takes the position that a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1530" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no-match letter is a distinct indication that </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1544" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the subject employee is not authorized to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1558" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in the United States. The regulation </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1572" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">creates an expansive definition of the term </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1586" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúconstructive knowledge‚Äù as applied to an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1600" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs information about an individual‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1614" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work in the United States </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1628" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the Immigration and Nationality Act.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1642" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1656" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An employer may violate federal regulations </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1670" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">if it has knowledge that an employee is an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1684" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker. An employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1698" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">deemed to have knowledge if a reasonable </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1712" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person would infer from the facts that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1726" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee is unauthorized. Constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1740" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge can be found where one of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1754" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following is true:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1768" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1782" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The I-9 form employment eligibility form has </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1796" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not been properly completed (including </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1810" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">support documentation).</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1824" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer has learned that the worker is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1838" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not authorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1852" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1866" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer acts with reckless disregard </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1880" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for the legal consequences or permitting </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1894" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">another individual to introduce an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1908" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized worker into the workforce.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1922" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Examples of an employer‚Äôs constructive </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1936" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge that an employee may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1950" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work include:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1964" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1978" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Social Security </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="1992" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Administration that the combination of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2006" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">name and social security number submitted </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2020" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for an employee do not match agency </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2034" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2048" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">written notice from the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2062" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security that the immigration </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2076" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status document or employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2090" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization document presented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2104" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referenced by the employee in completing </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2118" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9 was assigned to another person or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2132" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the agency has no record that the document </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2146" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has been assigned</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2160" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a request by a worker (who already claimed </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2174" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to be a permanent resident, U.S. citizen or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2188" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. national) that the employer file an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2202" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant labor certification or employment-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2216" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">based immigration visa petition.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2230" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The amended regulation also describes </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2244" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúsafe harbor‚Äù procedures that the employer </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2258" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">can follow in response to such a letter and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2272" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">thereby be certain that the Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2286" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Homeland Security will not use the letter as </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2300" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">part of an allegation that the employer had </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2314" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">constructive knowledge that the employee </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2328" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">referred to in the letter is an immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2342" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">unauthorized to work within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2356" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States.¬† The ‚Äúsafe harbor‚Äù procedures </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2370" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">include attempting to resolve the no-match </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2384" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">issue and, if it cannot be resolved within a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2398" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certain period of time, independently </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2412" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verifying the employee‚Äôs identity and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2426" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment authorization through a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2440" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialized process.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2454" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2468" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigration and Customs Enforcement </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2482" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">considers employers to have acted </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2496" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reasonably if the employer resolves the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2510" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancy with the relevant agency within </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2524" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">30 days of receiving a no match letter by </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2538" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">doing all of the following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2552" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2566" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">checking its records for a clerical error</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2580" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">informing the agency of its error</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2594" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">verifying that the name and number, as </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2608" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">corrected, match the agency‚Äôs records.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2622" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employer cannot resolve the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2636" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">discrepancy as described above, it must </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2650" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">contact the employee and request </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2664" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">confirmation that the employee‚Äôs information </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2678" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is correct. If the original information was </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2692" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct, the employer must do all of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2706" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2720" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2734" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct the employee‚Äôs information in its </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2748" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">records</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2762" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">inform the relevant agency of the correction</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2776" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">match the corrected information with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2790" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">agency‚Äôs records.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2804" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If the employee who is the subject of a no-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2818" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">match letter maintains that the information </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2832" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">he or she provided to the employer is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2846" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">correct, the employer must ask the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2860" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee to pursue the matter him or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2874" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">herself with the agency. Employers who </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2888" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">take these corrective steps within 30 days of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2902" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">receiving a no-match letter are regarded as </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2916" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">having acted reasonably and fall within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2930" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">safe-harbor.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2944" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2958" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Likewise, many states have laws making it </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2972" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">illegal for an employer to knowingly employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="2986" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or refer for employment any individual who </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3000" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">has illegally entered the United States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3014" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3028">Temporary visas</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3042" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3056" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. employers may sponsor foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3070" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employees for certain temporary </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3084" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa¬†categories that authorize employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3098" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in this country. Some of these categories </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3112" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">include:¬†</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3126" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3140" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B ‚Äì Specialty occupation (professional)</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3154" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3168" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B visa is for professionals who will </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3182" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">work in a ‚Äúspecialty occupation‚Äù on a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3196" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary basis for no more than six years. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3210" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The duration of stay is three years, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3224" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">extendable to six years. An exception to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3238" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">maximum length of stay applies in certain </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3252" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">circumstances. A specialty occupation is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3266" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">one that requires:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3280" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3294" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">theoretical and practical application of a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3308" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">body of highly specialized knowledge</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3322" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">attainment of a bachelor‚Äôs or higher degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3336" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in the specific specialty (or its equivalent) as </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3350" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a minimum for entry into the occupation in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3364" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3378" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are numerous occupations that </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3392" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">potentially qualify as specialty occupations. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3406" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer must prove -- through </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3420" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">objective evidence -- that the job offered </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3434" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">falls within the statutory and regulatory </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3448" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">definitions set forth.¬† Typical occupations </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3462" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualifying for H1B visa status include </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3476" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professions, which are defined by INA </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3490" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬ß101(a)(32) to include architects, engineers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3504" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">lawyers, physicians, surgeons and teachers </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3518" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in elementary or secondary schools, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3532" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">colleges, academies or seminaries. H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3546" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visas are employer and job specific.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3560" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3574" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Current laws limit the annual number of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3588" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualifying foreign workers who may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3602" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">issued a visa or otherwise be provided H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3616" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status to 65,000 with an additional 20,000 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3630" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">under the H-1B advanced degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3644" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">exemption.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3658" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3672" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B1 (Chile and Singapore) program </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3686" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">allows employers to temporarily employ </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3700" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign workers from Chile and Singapore in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3714" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States on a nonimmigrant basis </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3728" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in specialty occupations. Current laws limit </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3742" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the annual number of qualifying foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3756" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">workers who may be issued an H-1B1 visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3770" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to 6,800 with 1,400 from Chile and 5,400 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3784" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">from Singapore.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3798" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3812" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-1B petition process involves </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3826" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certification of a labor condition </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3840" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">application¬†(LCA) by the U.S. Department of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3854" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Labor (DOL) and approval of an H-1B visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3868" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition filed with the USCIS. Employers </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3882" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must submit an LCA to the DOL </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3896" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">electronically through the FLAG system </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3910" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">attesting to compliance with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3924" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirements of H-1B or H-1B1. LCAs must </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3938" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not be submitted more than six months </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3952" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before the beginning date of the period of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3966" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment. The two exceptions to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3980" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">electronic filing are employers with physical </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="3994" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">disabilities or those who lack Internet </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4008" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">access and cannot electronically file the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4022" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form ETA-9035E. An employer must </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4036" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition the administrator of OFLC for prior </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4050" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">special permission to file an LCA by mail on </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4064" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the Form ETA-9035.¬† After the employer‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4078" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B petition is approved by USCIS, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4092" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">individual worker can obtain an H-1B visa </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4106" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">stamp by appointment at the U.S. consulate </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4120" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or embassy in his or her native country. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4134" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the individual is already in the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4148" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States, a change of status to H-1B is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4162" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">possible; and if the individual is already in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4176" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B status, he or she can begin working </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4190" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for a new H-1B employer as soon as the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4204" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer‚Äôs petition is filed without having to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4218" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">wait for an approval. The LCA verification </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4232" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">process requires the employer to certify that </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4246" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4260" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4274" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B individual will be paid the higher of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4288" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">prevailing or actual wage for that occupation </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4302" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in the area of intended employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4316" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will offer the individual the same </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4330" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">terms and conditions of employment that it </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4344" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offers to U.S. workers</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4358" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment of the noncitizen will not </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4372" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">adversely affect the wages and working </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4386" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">conditions of workers similarly employed in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4400" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the area of intended employment</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4414" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will not employ the individual in a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4428" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">strike or lockout or work stoppage related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4442" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a labor dispute in the occupation at the time </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4456" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the application is signed</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4470" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer will notify other similarly situated </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4484" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employees (or their agent) of its intent to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4498" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employ an H-1B individual in the relevant </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4512" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">position.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4526" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer must also document its </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4540" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">compliance with the LCA verifications by </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4554" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">retaining relevant documents and by making </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4568" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available a ‚Äúpublic inspection‚Äù file upon </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4582" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">request.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4596" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4610" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-1B status is initially granted for no more </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4624" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">than three years. Extensions are available, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4638" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">but the employee is subject to a maximum </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4652" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">cumulative period of six years of H-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4666" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status. H-1B extensions beyond the six-year </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4680" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">limit are possible if the individual is the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4694" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">beneficiary of an employment-based </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4708" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence process that has been </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4722" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">pending for more than one year or is the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4736" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">beneficiary of an approved immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4750" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition and is unable to adjust status to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4764" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence because of per-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4778" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country limits.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4792" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4806" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The employer will be liable for the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4820" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reasonable costs of the foreign national's </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4834" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">return transportation if the employer </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4848" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">terminates the foreign national before the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4862" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">end of the foreign national's period of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4876" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorized stay. The employer is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4890" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">responsible for the costs of foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4904" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">national's return transportation if foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4918" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">national voluntarily resigns the position.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4932" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4946" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Treaty NAFTA ‚Äì Canadian and Mexican </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4960" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professionals</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4974" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="4988" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Under the North American Free Trade </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5002" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Agreement¬†(NAFTA), citizens of Canada </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5016" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and Mexico who are qualified professionals </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5030" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">can work in the United States using the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5044" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Treaty NAFTA or TN, classification. This </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5058" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa category is available for designated </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5072" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">professional occupations set forth in an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5086" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">appendix to NAFTA. The list of professions </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5100" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">includes many occupations that would also </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5114" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">qualify for H-1 status, such as engineers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5128" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">accountants and professors. One advantage </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5142" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of TN status is that the application </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5156" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure is very simple. An applicant can </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5170" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">apply at the border by presenting all of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5184" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">following:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5198" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5212" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">proof of Canadian or Mexican citizenship</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5226" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">proof of membership in a listed occupation</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5240" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an offer of employment in that occupation </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5254" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">from a U.S. employer</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5268" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$50.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5282" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The ‚Äúapplication‚Äù is adjudicated on-the-spot </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5296" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and, if approved, the immigrant is given a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5310" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">multiple-entry TN status good for one year.¬†¬†</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5324" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5338" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Although TN status can theoretically be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5352" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">renewed indefinitely in one-year increments </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5366" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a petition or by reapplying at the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5380" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">border, in practice the status may be limited </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5394" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to five or six years of renewals because the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5408" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">treaty states that TN status cannot be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5422" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted to an immigrant who intends to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5436" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">reside in the United States permanently. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5450" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of TN immigrants can get TD </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5464" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Treaty Dependent) status but cannot use </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5478" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that status to work in this country.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5492" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5506" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1A and L-1B ‚Äì Intracompany transfers of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5520" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managers/executives or specialized </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5534" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge personnel</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5548" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5562" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The L-1A¬†and L-1B visas are designed to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5576" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">facilitate the temporary transfer of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5590" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managerial, executive and specialized </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5604" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowledge personnel from overseas entities </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5618" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to related U.S. entities. L-1A status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5632" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">managers and executives and L-1B status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5646" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for persons with specialized knowledge of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5660" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company methods, products, procedures, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5674" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">operations, etc. To qualify for L-1 status, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5688" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employee must have worked for the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5702" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">company abroad in a managerial, executive </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5716" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or specialized knowledge position for at </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5730" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">least one full year during the three years </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5744" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">prior to the transfer to a managerial, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5758" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executive or specialized knowledge position </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5772" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">with the related U.S. entity. First line </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5786" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">supervisors are not eligible for L-1A status </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5800" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">as managers unless the persons they </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5814" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">supervise are professionals.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5828" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5842" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The U.S. employer must file a petition for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5856" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1 status with the regional USCIS Service </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5870" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Center with jurisdiction over the location </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5884" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">where the immigrant will work. Canadian </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5898" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferees may submit the petition at the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5912" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S.-Canada border for immediate </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5926" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">adjudication. Once the employer‚Äôs petition is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5940" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">approved, the immigrant may obtain an L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5954" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa stamp from the U.S. embassy or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5968" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">consulate abroad or if already in the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5982" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States, may commence the L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="5996" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6010" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6024" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">L-1 status is initially granted for three years </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6038" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and extensions are available for two-year </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6052" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">periods. L-1A managers/executives are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6066" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entitled to up to seven years of L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6080" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment in the United States and L-1B </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6094" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialized knowledge personnel are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6108" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">eligible for a maximum of five years of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6122" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorized stay. Dependents of L-1 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6136" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferees obtain L-2 status. Unlike most </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6150" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary visa categories that do not allow </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6164" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependents to work, L-2 spouses may </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6178" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">obtain employment authorization.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6192" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6206" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Some multi-national companies may qualify </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6220" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for ‚Äúblanket‚Äù L-1 status. Typically, this is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6234" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available for entities that transfer more than </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6248" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">10 people per year, have annual sales in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6262" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">excess of $25 million or more than 1,000 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6276" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. employees. Blanket L-1 status allows </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6290" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. entity to bypass the USCIS petition </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6304" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">process in individual cases. Instead, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6318" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. entity sends a special form to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6332" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">transferee, who then applies for L-1 status </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6346" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">directly at the U.S. consulate or embassy.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6360" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6374" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1 and E-2 ‚Äì Treaty trader/investor</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6388" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6402" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Based upon a bilateral investment treaty or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6416" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">a treaty of friendship, navigation and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6430" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commerce between the United States and a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6444" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign country, an individual may come to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6458" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the United States to open and operate a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6472" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign-owned business or be employed in a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6486" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">foreign-owned business that already exists </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6500" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">here. Entities engaged in substantial trade </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6514" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">between the United States and the treaty </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6528" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country will be able to transfer managers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6542" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives and key personnel using the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6556" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1¬†(Treaty Trader) visa status. Entities </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6570" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">making a substantial investment in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6584" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States may transfer managers, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6598" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives and key personnel using the E-2 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6612" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">(Treaty Investor) visa status.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6626" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6640" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The foreign entity must be a ‚Äúcitizen‚Äù or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6654" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚Äúnative‚Äù of the treaty country. This means </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6668" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that at least a majority of the ownership of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6682" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the foreign entity must be held by citizens of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6696" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the treaty country. The person seeking E </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6710" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa status must also be a citizen of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6724" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">treaty country. There is no prior employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6738" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirement, however.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6752" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6766" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">E-1 immigrants must be engaged in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6780" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">activities supporting a substantial volume of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6794" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">international trade in goods or services. E-2 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6808" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants must be directing or developing </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6822" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an active and substantial investment of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6836" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">irrevocably committed funds devoted to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6850" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">production of goods or services. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6864" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">‚ÄúSubstantial‚Äù means more than enough to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6878" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">secure the success of the enterprise and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6892" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">more than enough to support the E </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6906" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant and family members.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6920" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6934" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Most E immigrants apply for E visa status </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6948" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">directly at the U.S. embassy or consulate in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6962" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the treaty country, but it is possible to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6976" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">change to E status from within the United </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="6990" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">States Immigrants admitted in E status are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7004" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted two years of authorized stay so long </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7018" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">as their E visa stamp is valid at the time of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7032" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entry. Typically, E visas are valid for five </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7046" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">years, but this may vary depending upon </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7060" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the terms of the treaty. In most cases, the E </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7074" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa can be renewed for additional periods </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7088" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">provided that the underlying trade or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7102" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">investment remains viable.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7116" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7130" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of E visa immigrants acquire </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7144" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the same status as the principal immigrant, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7158" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">such as E-1 or E-2 status. E-2 spouses may </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7172" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">obtain employment authorization.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7186" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7200" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2A and H-2B ‚Äì Agricultural and other </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7214" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">seasonal and temporary workers</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7228" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7242" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The H-2A visa¬†is for seasonal agricultural </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7256" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">workers and the H-2B visa¬†is for non-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7270" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">agricultural temporary or seasonal workers. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7284" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2 status is only available for jobs that are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7298" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">truly temporary in nature, so the status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7312" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">almost always limited to one year. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7326" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer must test the market for available </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7340" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. workers and obtain a certification from </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7354" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">DOL that none are available to fill the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7368" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">temporary position(s). The test of the market </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7382" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must offer prevailing wages and working </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7396" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">conditions.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7410" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7424" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There is a quota or limit on the number of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7438" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2B visas that can be issued each fiscal </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7452" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">year. Often, the quota is exhausted well </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7466" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before the end of the fiscal year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7480" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7494" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-2A employers may be required to hire </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7508" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. workers who apply for work anytime up </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7522" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to halfway through the certification period, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7536" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">even if that involves discharging the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7550" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant worker. Also, H-2A employers </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7564" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">may need to pay special wages, offer </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7578" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">housing and in some cases may have to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7592" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">pay transportation costs for the immigrant to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7606" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">come to the work site and return home.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7620" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
