                <tspan x="36" y="7634" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Each H-2 period of authorized stay will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7648" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">one year or less. After using three </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7662" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">consecutive H-2 periods, the immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7676" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must remain outside the United States for at </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7690" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">least six months before becoming eligible to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7704" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">use H-2 status again.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7718" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7732" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">H-3 ‚ÄìTrainees</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7746" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7760" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">A U.S. employer may sponsor an immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7774" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for H-3¬†status to provide the immigrant </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7788" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training that is unavailable in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7802" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs native country. The immigrant is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7816" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">not supposed to engage in productive </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7830" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training other than as necessary to provide </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7844" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">effective training. H-3 immigrants cannot </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7858" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">displace U.S. workers. The petitioning </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7872" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer must supply extensive </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7886" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">documentation of an appropriate training </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7900" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">curriculum with the petition. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7914" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">documentation must specifically discuss the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7928" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">amount of on-the-job vs. classroom training, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7942" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">address why the training is not available in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7956" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the trainee‚Äôs native country and explain how </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7970" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the training experience will enhance the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7984" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs career prospects abroad. H-3 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="7998" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status is limited to the duration of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8012" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training program, which cannot exceed two </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8026" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">years.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8040" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8054" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-1 ‚ÄìAcademic students</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8068" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8082" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-l visas¬†are for students engaged in degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8096" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">programs at U.S. academic institutions. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8110" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are several types of employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8124" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization available to F-l foreign </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8138" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">students, including on-campus employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8152" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">off-campus employment due to severe </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8166" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">economic hardship, international </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8180" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">organization internships, curricular practical </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8194" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training and optional practical training </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8208" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">before and after completion of studies.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8222" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8236" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An F-l student engaged in a full course of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8250" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">study may engage in part-time on-campus </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8264" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment such as working in a cafeteria </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8278" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or bookstore so long as this employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8292" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">does not displace a U.S. worker. This type </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8306" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">of on-campus employment does not require </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8320" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">advance permission from USCIS.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8334" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8348" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">An F-l student may apply for employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8362" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization to work off-campus due to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8376" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">economic necessity or for an internship with </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8390" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an international organization. Economic </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8404" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">necessity work permits are normally not </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8418" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted except upon proof of a substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8432" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and unforeseen change in the student‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8446" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">finances.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8460" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8474" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-1 students may also engage in practical </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8488" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training employment related to their degree </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8502" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">program. While enrolled, F-1 students may </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8516" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">use Curricular Practical Training. This may </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8530" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">take the form of an internship, co-op, work-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8544" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">study program or some other activity that is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8558" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">an integral part of the degree program and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8572" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">CPT can be commenced upon an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8586" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">endorsement by the school‚Äôs foreign student </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8600" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">advisor. A student who uses more than 12 </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8614" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">months of CPT becomes ineligible for post-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8628" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">graduate Optional Practical Training¬†(OPT).</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8642" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8656" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">OPT permits up to 12 months of on-the-job </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8670" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">practical training upon completion of an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8684" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">academic degree program. F-1 students </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8698" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">must apply for a work permit in order to use </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8712" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">OPT and cannot commence employment </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8726" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">until the permit is issued.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8740" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8754" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Dependents of F-1 immigrants are granted </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8768" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">F-2 status and cannot work.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8782" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8796" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">J-1 ‚ÄìExchange visitors</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8810" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8824" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrants participating in a designated </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8838" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">exchange visitor program may engage in </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8852" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specific types of employment as part of their </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8866" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">program activities. There are many types of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8880" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">J-1 exchange visitor programs, including </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8894" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">those for students, practical trainees, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8908" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">teachers, professors, research assistants, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8922" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">specialists, camp counselors, au pairs and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8936" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">distinguished visitors. J-1 practical trainees </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8950" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">are authorized up to 18 months of on-the-</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8964" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">job training; other categories have different </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8978" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">time limits.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="8992" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9006" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Some exchange visitors are subject to a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9020" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">two-year home country residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9034" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">requirement that must be satisfied before </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9048" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant is eligible for H, L or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9062" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent resident status. This obligation </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9076" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">arises if the immigrant‚Äôs exchange visit is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9090" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">funded by the immigrant‚Äôs government or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9104" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. government, if the immigrant‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9118" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">skills are in short supply in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9132" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">country or if the immigrant is coming to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9146" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States to obtain graduate medical </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9160" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">education. If the immigrant is subject to the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9174" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">two-year residence requirement, so too are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9188" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">all of the immigrant‚Äôs dependents. It is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9202" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sometimes possible to obtain a waiver of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9216" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">this requirement, but the waiver process is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9230" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">cumbersome and time-consuming.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9244" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9258" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">O ‚ÄìExtraordinary ability immigrants</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9272" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9286" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The O category is for highly talented or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9300" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">acclaimed individuals who are scientists, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9314" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">educators, artists, athletes, entertainers or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9328" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">business people. To qualify for O </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9342" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">visa¬†status, the immigrant must demonstrate </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9356" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sustained national or international acclaim. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9370" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The U.S. employer must show that the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9384" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant will fill a position that requires a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9398" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">person of extraordinary ability. The </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9412" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petitioning employer must also submit a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9426" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">peer review evaluation confirming the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9440" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs international renown and the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9454" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">need for such a person. Typically, O status </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9468" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">will be granted for the duration of need but </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9482" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">no more than three years.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9496" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9510" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">P ‚ÄìPerforming artists, athletes and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9524" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">entertainers</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9538" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9552" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">P visa status is for performing artists, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9566" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">athletes and entertainers. Immigrants </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9580" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">seeking this category must demonstrate </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9594" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial achievement in their field. This </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9608" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status also requires a peer review </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9622" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">evaluation confirming the immigrant‚Äôs </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9636" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">international renown. P-1¬†status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9650" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">principal immigrants; P-2 status is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9664" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">essential supporting personnel; P-3 status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9678" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for coaches and trainers; and P-4 status is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9692" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for dependents. Generally, P visa status will </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9706" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">be granted for the duration of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9720" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">engagement or season.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9734" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9748" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employees gaining permanent residence</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9762" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9776" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">There are two major avenues to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9790" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent¬†residence:</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9804" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9818" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">family based sponsorship</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9832" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment-based sponsorship.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9846" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Each type of sponsorship has several </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9860" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">categories and different procedures.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9874" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9888" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Immigrants who marry U.S. citizens may be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9902" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">sponsored immediately for permanent </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9916" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residence and are not subject to category or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9930" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">per-country quotas. If the sponsor‚Äôs petition </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9944" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is filed within two years after the marriage, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9958" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant will be granted a conditional </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9972" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">permanent residence and the couple must </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="9986" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">file a joint petition to remove conditions on </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10000" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residence two years after the immigrant is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10014" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">granted conditional permanent residence. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10028" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">This requirement is intended to deter </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10042" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">marriage fraud.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10056" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10070" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Almost all other family-based petitions are </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10084" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">subject to category and per-country quotas </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10098" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and because of the high level of demand, it </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10112" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">may take many years before a visa is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10126" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">available. There are family-based categories </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10140" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">for unmarried sons and daughters of U.S. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10154" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">citizens, spouses and children of permanent </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10168" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">residents, married sons and daughters of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10182" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. citizens and brothers and sisters of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10196" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">U.S. citizens.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10210" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10224" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10238" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">also has several categories. Each has </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10252" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">different requirements. For some categories, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10266" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer must obtain ‚Äúlabor </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10280" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">certification,‚Äù such as a certification from </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10294" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">DOL that there are no U.S. workers qualified </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10308" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">and available to fill the position for which the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10322" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant is sponsored.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10336" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10350" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 1</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10364" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10378" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 1 is for Priority </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10392" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Workers, which includes Nobel laureates, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10406" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">college/university teachers/researchers and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10420" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">intracompany transferee managers/</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10434" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">executives. Labor certification is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10448" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">required for this category.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10462" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10476" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 2</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10490" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10504" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 2 is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10518" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants with advanced degrees and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10532" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrants with exceptional ability in the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10546" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">arts, sciences, education, athletics or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10560" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">business. Labor certification is usually </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10574" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">required for this category unless the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10588" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immigrant‚Äôs employment will directly serve </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10602" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">important U.S. interests.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10616" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10630" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 3</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10644" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10658" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 3 is the most </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10672" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">common of the employment-based </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10686" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">categories, as it is used by professionals </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10700" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">without advanced degrees, skilled workers </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10714" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">in jobs requiring at least two years of </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10728" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">training or education and unskilled workers. </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10742" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Labor certification is always required for this </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10756" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">category.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10770" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10784" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Categories 4 and 5</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10798" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10812" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Employment-based Category 4 is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10826" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Religious Workers, but is little-used now </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10840" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">because of a history of abuse. Similarly, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10854" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment-based Category 5, which is for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10868" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">investors committing more than $1.8 million </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10882" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">to the U.S. economy, is also little-used </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10896" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">because of a history of visa fraud.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10910" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10924" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Once labor certification is obtained, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10938" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer files a permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10952" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">petition with CIS. The immigrant and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10966" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">dependent family members may </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10980" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">concurrently file for adjustment of status. If </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="10994" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the immigrant has worked without </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11008" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">authorization or failed to maintain lawful </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11022" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">status at all times or if a visa is not </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11036" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">immediately available, the immigrant must </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11050" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">complete the permanent residence </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11064" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">procedure through consular processing at </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11078" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the U.S. embassy or consulate in his or her </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11092" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">native country.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11106" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11120" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The lawful resident verification information </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11134" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">is the documentation that is required by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11148" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">United States when completing the federal </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11162" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Form I-9.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11176" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11190" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">The penalties for employers</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11204" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11218" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If an employer knowingly hires, recruits or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11232" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">refers an undocumented immigrant for </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11246" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employment and a state or local </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11260" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">government agency has reason to believe </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11274" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">that a violation¬†has occurred, the agency is </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11288" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">mandated by law to file a complaint, which </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11302" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">triggers an automatic investigation by the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11316" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the commissioner finds </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11330" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">substantial evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11344" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">knowingly violated the law with respect to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11358" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">hiring, recruiting or referring an </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11372" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">undocumented immigrant for employment, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11386" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the commissioner will conduct a contested </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11400" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">case hearing. If the commissioner </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11414" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">determines that there is clear and </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11428" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">convincing evidence that an employer has </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11442" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">violated the law and the violation occurred </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11456" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">while the employer was acting within the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11470" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">parameters of the employer‚Äôs state issued </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11484" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">license, the appropriate regulatory board or </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11498" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the local government will revoke, suspend </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11512" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">or deny the employer‚Äôs license.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11526" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11540" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">If employers do not complete and retain the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11554" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">I-9 form properly, they may face civil money </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11568" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">penalties and possibly criminal penalties as </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11582" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">well. Fines for I-9 problems and document </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11596" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">abuse discrimination range from $234 to </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11610" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">$2,332. Penalties for knowingly employing </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11624" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">someone who lacks authorization to work </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11638" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">range from $583 to $4,666 for a first </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11652" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense, $4,667 to $11,663 for a second </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11666" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense and $6,999 to $23,333 for a third </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11680" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">offense. If a person is a federal contractor, </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11694" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">they may face debarment for substantial </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11708" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">noncompliance.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11722" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11736" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">Following an employer‚Äôs first violation, the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11750" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">regulatory board or local government will </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11764" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspend the employer‚Äôs license until the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11778" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">employer shows to the commissioner that </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11792" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">the employer is no longer in violation of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11806" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">¬†law. The employer may make this showing </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11820" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">by filing a sworn statement with the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11834" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">commissioner. If the employer commits a </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11848" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">second violation within three years of the </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11862" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">first violation, the employer‚Äôs license will be </tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11876" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal">suspended for one year.</tspan>
                <tspan x="36" y="11890" font-family="Helvetica" font-weight="normal"></tspan>
            </text>

                        <g transform="translate(205.000000, 23.000000)" id="cart">
                            <rect id="Rectangle" fill="#111111" x="0" y="0" width="17" height="17"></rect>
                            <ellipse id="Oval-Copy" stroke="#FFFFFF" stroke-width="0.75" cx="13.4181814" cy="13.752428" rx="1.71825101" ry="1.75166412"></ellipse>
                            <ellipse id="Oval-Copy-2" stroke="#FFFFFF" stroke-width="0.75" cx="6.440678" cy="13.752428" rx="1.71825101" ry="1.75166412"></ellipse>

            <text id="Welcome-to-the-Feder" font-family="Helvetica" font-size="10" font-weight="normal" letter-spacing="0.075000003" fill="#FFFFFF">
                <tspan x="39" y="119">Welcome to the Federal Human Resources Manual. </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="131">This guide contains details to help you comply with </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="143">federal employment laws. Please note that there are </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="155">also many state laws and ordinances related to </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="167">managing your employees ‚Äì if you are looking for a </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="179">complete guide to state and federal laws and </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="191">regulations, visit our resources page to find the what </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="203">is available in your state. Our state-specific Human </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="215">Resources Manuals provide a complete resource for </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="227">all of the employment-related laws affecting your </tspan>
                <tspan x="39" y="239">business operations.</tspan>
            </text>
